\hypertarget{config_config_format}{}\doxysection{Format}\label{config_config_format}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} configuration file is a free-\/form A\+S\+C\+II text file with a structure that is similar to that of a {\ttfamily Makefile}, with the default name {\ttfamily Doxyfile}. It is parsed by {\ttfamily doxygen}. The file may contain tabs and newlines for formatting purposes. The statements in the file are case-\/sensitive. Comments may be placed anywhere within the file (except within quotes). Comments beginning with two hash characters ({\ttfamily \#\#}) are kept when updating the configuration file and are placed in front of the T\+AG they are in front of. Comments beginning with two hash characters ({\ttfamily \#\#}) at the beginning of the configuration file are also kept and placed at the beginning of the file. Comments beginning with two hash characters ({\ttfamily \#\#}) at the end of the configuration file are also kept and placed at the end of the file. Comments begin with the hash character ({\ttfamily \#}) and ends at the end of the line.

The file essentially consists of a list of assignment statements. Each statement consists of a {\ttfamily T\+A\+G\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} written in capitals, followed by the equal sign ({\ttfamily =}) and one or more values. If the same tag is assigned more than once, the last assignment overwrites any earlier assignment. For tags that take a list as their argument, the {\ttfamily +=} operator can be used instead of {\ttfamily =} to append new values to the list. Values are sequences of non-\/blanks. If the value should contain one or more blanks it must be surrounded by quotes ({\ttfamily "..."}). Multiple lines can be concatenated by inserting a backslash ({\ttfamily \textbackslash{}}) as the last character of a line. Environment variables can be expanded using the pattern {\ttfamily \$(E\+N\+V\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME)}.

You can also include part of a configuration file from another configuration file using a {\ttfamily @I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+DE} tag as follows\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}@INCLUDE = config_file_name
\end{DoxyVerb}
 The include file is searched in the current working directory. You can also specify a list of directories that should be searched before looking in the current working directory. Do this by putting a {\ttfamily @I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag with these paths before the {\ttfamily @I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+DE} tag, e.\+g.\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}@INCLUDE_PATH = my_config_dir
\end{DoxyVerb}


The configuration options can be divided into several categories. Below is an alphabetical index of the tags that are recognized followed by the descriptions of the tags grouped by category. \footnotesize

\item \contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_strict_proto_matching}{S\+T\+R\+I\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+C\+H\+I\+NG}}}{\ref{config_cfg_strict_proto_matching}}{}
\item \contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_strip_code_comments}{S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+E\+N\+TS}}}{\ref{config_cfg_strip_code_comments}}{}
\item \contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_strip_from_inc_path}{S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}}}{\ref{config_cfg_strip_from_inc_path}}{}
\item \contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_strip_from_path}{S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}}}{\ref{config_cfg_strip_from_path}}{}

\item \contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_uml_limit_num_fields}{U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+I\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+F\+I\+E\+L\+DS}}}{\ref{config_cfg_uml_limit_num_fields}}{}

\end{multicols}
\normalsize
 \hypertarget{config_config_project}{}\doxysection{Project related configuration options}\label{config_config_project}
\label{config_cfg_doxyfile_encoding}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_doxyfile_encoding}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+X\+Y\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG} ]\index{DOXYFILE\_ENCODING@{DOXYFILE\_ENCODING}} This tag specifies the encoding used for all characters in the configuration file that follow. The default is U\+T\+F-\/8 which is also the encoding used for all text before the first occurrence of this tag. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} uses {\ttfamily libiconv} (or the iconv built into {\ttfamily libc}) for the transcoding. See \href{https://www.gnu.org/software/libiconv/}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+gnu.\+org/software/libiconv/}} for the list of possible encodings.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily U\+T\+F-\/8}.

\label{config_cfg_project_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_project_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{PROJECT\_NAME@{PROJECT\_NAME}} The {\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag is a single word (or a sequence of words surrounded by double-\/quotes, unless you are using Doxywizard) that should identify the project for which the documentation is generated. This name is used in the title of most generated pages and in a few other places.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily My Project}.

\label{config_cfg_project_number}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_project_number}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER} ]\index{PROJECT\_NUMBER@{PROJECT\_NUMBER}} The {\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER} tag can be used to enter a project or revision number. This could be handy for archiving the generated documentation or if some version control system is used.

\label{config_cfg_project_brief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_project_brief}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{PROJECT\_BRIEF@{PROJECT\_BRIEF}} Using the {\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} tag one can provide an optional one line description for a project that appears at the top of each page and should give viewer a quick idea about the purpose of the project. Keep the description short.

\label{config_cfg_project_logo}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_project_logo}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO} ]\index{PROJECT\_LOGO@{PROJECT\_LOGO}} With the {\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO} tag one can specify a logo or an icon that is included in the documentation. The maximum height of the logo should not exceed 55 pixels and the maximum width should not exceed 200 pixels. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will copy the logo to the output directory.

\label{config_cfg_output_directory}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_output_directory}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY} ]\index{OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY@{OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY}} The {\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY} tag is used to specify the (relative or absolute) path into which the generated documentation will be written. If a relative path is entered, it will be relative to the location where doxygen was started. If left blank the current directory will be used.

\label{config_cfg_create_subdirs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_create_subdirs}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+D\+I\+RS} ]\index{CREATE\_SUBDIRS@{CREATE\_SUBDIRS}} If the {\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+D\+I\+RS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will create 4096 sub-\/directories (in 2 levels) under the output directory of each output format and will distribute the generated files over these directories. Enabling this option can be useful when feeding doxygen a huge amount of source files, where putting all generated files in the same directory would otherwise causes performance problems for the file system.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_allow_unicode_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_allow_unicode_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{ALLOW\_UNICODE\_NAMES@{ALLOW\_UNICODE\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will allow non-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II characters to appear in the names of generated files. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, non-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II characters will be escaped, for example \+\_\+x\+E3\+\_\+x81\+\_\+x84 will be used for Unicode U+3044.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_output_language}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_output_language}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+N\+G\+U\+A\+GE} ]\index{OUTPUT\_LANGUAGE@{OUTPUT\_LANGUAGE}} The {\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+N\+G\+U\+A\+GE} tag is used to specify the language in which all documentation generated by doxygen is written. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will use this information to generate all constant output in the proper language.

Possible values are\+: {\ttfamily Afrikaans}, {\ttfamily Arabic}, {\ttfamily Armenian}, {\ttfamily Brazilian}, {\ttfamily Catalan}, {\ttfamily Chinese}, {\ttfamily Chinese-\/\+Traditional}, {\ttfamily Croatian}, {\ttfamily Czech}, {\ttfamily Danish}, {\ttfamily Dutch}, {\ttfamily English} (United States), {\ttfamily Esperanto}, {\ttfamily Farsi} (Persian), {\ttfamily Finnish}, {\ttfamily French}, {\ttfamily German}, {\ttfamily Greek}, {\ttfamily Hungarian}, {\ttfamily Indonesian}, {\ttfamily Italian}, {\ttfamily Japanese}, {\ttfamily Japanese-\/en} (Japanese with English messages), {\ttfamily Korean}, {\ttfamily Korean-\/en} (Korean with English messages), {\ttfamily Latvian}, {\ttfamily Lithuanian}, {\ttfamily Macedonian}, {\ttfamily Norwegian}, {\ttfamily Persian} (Farsi), {\ttfamily Polish}, {\ttfamily Portuguese}, {\ttfamily Romanian}, {\ttfamily Russian}, {\ttfamily Serbian}, {\ttfamily Serbian-\/\+Cyrillic}, {\ttfamily Slovak}, {\ttfamily Slovene}, {\ttfamily Spanish}, {\ttfamily Swedish}, {\ttfamily Turkish}, {\ttfamily Ukrainian} and {\ttfamily Vietnamese}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily English}.

\label{config_cfg_output_text_direction}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_output_text_direction}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON} ]\index{OUTPUT\_TEXT\_DIRECTION@{OUTPUT\_TEXT\_DIRECTION}} The {\ttfamily O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON} tag is used to specify the direction in which all documentation generated by doxygen is written. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will use this information to generate all generated output in the proper direction.

Possible values are\+: {\ttfamily None}, {\ttfamily L\+TR}, {\ttfamily R\+TL} and {\ttfamily Context}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily None}.

\label{config_cfg_brief_member_desc}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_brief_member_desc}%

\item[{\ttfamily B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+SC} ]\index{BRIEF\_MEMBER\_DESC@{BRIEF\_MEMBER\_DESC}} If the {\ttfamily B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+SC} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will include brief member descriptions after the members that are listed in the file and class documentation (similar to {\ttfamily Javadoc}). Set to {\ttfamily NO} to disable this.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_repeat_brief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_repeat_brief}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+E\+P\+E\+A\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{REPEAT\_BRIEF@{REPEAT\_BRIEF}} If the {\ttfamily R\+E\+P\+E\+A\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will prepend the brief description of a member or function before the detailed description ~\newline
Note\+: If both \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_hide_undoc_members}{H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+RS}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_brief_member_desc}{B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+SC}} are set to {\ttfamily NO}, the brief descriptions will be completely suppressed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_abbreviate_brief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_abbreviate_brief}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+B\+B\+R\+E\+V\+I\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{ABBREVIATE\_BRIEF@{ABBREVIATE\_BRIEF}} This tag implements a quasi-\/intelligent brief description abbreviator that is used to form the text in various listings. Each string in this list, if found as the leading text of the brief description, will be stripped from the text and the result, after processing the whole list, is used as the annotated text. Otherwise, the brief description is used as-\/is. If left blank, the following values are used ({\ttfamily \$name} is automatically replaced with the name of the entity)\+: {\ttfamily The \$name class}, {\ttfamily The \$name widget}, {\ttfamily The \$name file}, {\ttfamily is}, {\ttfamily provides}, {\ttfamily specifies}, {\ttfamily contains}, {\ttfamily represents}, {\ttfamily a}, {\ttfamily an} and {\ttfamily the}.

\label{config_cfg_always_detailed_sec}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_always_detailed_sec}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+T\+A\+I\+L\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+EC} ]\index{ALWAYS\_DETAILED\_SEC@{ALWAYS\_DETAILED\_SEC}} If the {\ttfamily A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+T\+A\+I\+L\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+EC} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_repeat_brief}{R\+E\+P\+E\+A\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF}} tags are both set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a detailed section even if there is only a brief description.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_inline_inherited_memb}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inline_inherited_memb}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+H\+E\+R\+I\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+E\+MB} ]\index{INLINE\_INHERITED\_MEMB@{INLINE\_INHERITED\_MEMB}} If the {\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+H\+E\+R\+I\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+E\+MB} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will show all inherited members of a class in the documentation of that class as if those members were ordinary class members. Constructors, destructors and assignment operators of the base classes will not be shown.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_full_path_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_full_path_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+U\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{FULL\_PATH\_NAMES@{FULL\_PATH\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily F\+U\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will prepend the full path before files name in the file list and in the header files. If set to {\ttfamily NO} the shortest path that makes the file name unique will be used

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_strip_from_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_strip_from_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{STRIP\_FROM\_PATH@{STRIP\_FROM\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to strip a user-\/defined part of the path. Stripping is only done if one of the specified strings matches the left-\/hand part of the path. The tag can be used to show relative paths in the file list. If left blank the directory from which doxygen is run is used as the path to strip. ~\newline
Note that you can specify absolute paths here, but also relative paths, which will be relative from the directory where doxygen is started.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_full_path_names}{F\+U\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_strip_from_inc_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_strip_from_inc_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{STRIP\_FROM\_INC\_PATH@{STRIP\_FROM\_INC\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to strip a user-\/defined part of the path mentioned in the documentation of a class, which tells the reader which header file to include in order to use a class. If left blank only the name of the header file containing the class definition is used. Otherwise one should specify the list of include paths that are normally passed to the compiler using the {\ttfamily -\/I} flag.

\label{config_cfg_short_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_short_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{SHORT\_NAMES@{SHORT\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate much shorter (but less readable) file names. This can be useful is your file systems doesn\textquotesingle{}t support long names like on D\+OS, Mac, or C\+D-\/\+R\+OM.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_javadoc_autobrief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_javadoc_autobrief}%

\item[{\ttfamily J\+A\+V\+A\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{JAVADOC\_AUTOBRIEF@{JAVADOC\_AUTOBRIEF}} If the {\ttfamily J\+A\+V\+A\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+R\+I\+EF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will interpret the first line (until the first dot) of a Javadoc-\/style comment as the brief description. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the Javadoc-\/style will behave just like regular Qt-\/style comments (thus requiring an explicit @brief command for a brief description.)

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_javadoc_banner}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_javadoc_banner}%

\item[{\ttfamily J\+A\+V\+A\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+N\+N\+ER} ]\index{JAVADOC\_BANNER@{JAVADOC\_BANNER}} If the {\ttfamily J\+A\+V\+A\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+N\+N\+ER} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will interpret a line such as\begin{DoxyVerb}/***************\end{DoxyVerb}
 as being the beginning of a Javadoc-\/style comment \char`\"{}banner\char`\"{}. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the Javadoc-\/style will behave just like regular comments and it will not be interpreted by doxygen.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_qt_autobrief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qt_autobrief}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{QT\_AUTOBRIEF@{QT\_AUTOBRIEF}} If the {\ttfamily Q\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+R\+I\+EF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will interpret the first line (until the first dot) of a Qt-\/style comment as the brief description. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the Qt-\/style will behave just like regular Qt-\/style comments (thus requiring an explicit \textbackslash{}brief command for a brief description.)

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_multiline_cpp_is_brief}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_multiline_cpp_is_brief}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+P\+P\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} ]\index{MULTILINE\_CPP\_IS\_BRIEF@{MULTILINE\_CPP\_IS\_BRIEF}} The {\ttfamily M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+P\+P\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF} tag can be set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to make doxygen treat a multi-\/line C++ special comment block (i.\+e. a block of {\ttfamily //!} or {\ttfamily ///} comments) as a brief description. This used to be the default behavior. The new default is to treat a multi-\/line C++ comment block as a detailed description. Set this tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if you prefer the old behavior instead. ~\newline
Note that setting this tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} also means that rational rose comments are not recognized any more.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_inherit_docs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inherit_docs}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+H\+E\+R\+I\+T\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} ]\index{INHERIT\_DOCS@{INHERIT\_DOCS}} If the {\ttfamily I\+N\+H\+E\+R\+I\+T\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then an undocumented member inherits the documentation from any documented member that it re-\/implements.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_separate_member_pages}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_separate_member_pages}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES} ]\index{SEPARATE\_MEMBER\_PAGES@{SEPARATE\_MEMBER\_PAGES}} If the {\ttfamily S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will produce a new page for each member. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the documentation of a member will be part of the file/class/namespace that contains it.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_tab_size}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_tab_size}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+A\+B\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE} ]\index{TAB\_SIZE@{TAB\_SIZE}} The {\ttfamily T\+A\+B\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE} tag can be used to set the number of spaces in a tab. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} uses this value to replace tabs by spaces in code fragments.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 1}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 16}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 4}.

\label{config_cfg_aliases}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_aliases}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+ES} ]\index{ALIASES@{ALIASES}} This tag can be used to specify a number of aliases that act as commands in the documentation. An alias has the form\+: \begin{DoxyVerb} name=value
\end{DoxyVerb}
 For example adding \begin{DoxyVerb} "sideeffect=@par Side Effects:\n"
\end{DoxyVerb}
 will allow you to put the command {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}sideeffect} (or {\ttfamily @sideeffect}) in the documentation, which will result in a user-\/defined paragraph with heading \char`\"{}\+Side Effects\+:\char`\"{}. You can put \textbackslash{}n\textquotesingle{}s in the value part of an alias to insert newlines (in the resulting output). You can put {\ttfamily $^\wedge$$^\wedge$} in the value part of an alias to insert a newline as if a physical newline was in the original file. When you need a literal {\ttfamily \{} or {\ttfamily \}} or {\ttfamily ,} in the value part of an alias you have to escape them by means of a backslash ({\ttfamily \textbackslash{}}), this can lead to conflicts with the commands {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}\{} and {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}\}} for these it is advised to use the version {\ttfamily @\{} and {\ttfamily @\}} or use a double escape ({\ttfamily \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\{} and {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\}})

\label{config_cfg_tcl_subst}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_tcl_subst}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+C\+L\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+ST} ]\index{TCL\_SUBST@{TCL\_SUBST}} This tag can be used to specify a number of word-\/keyword mappings (T\+CL only). \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} mapping has the form {\ttfamily \char`\"{}name=value\char`\"{}}. For example adding {\ttfamily \char`\"{}class=itcl\+::class\char`\"{}} will allow you to use the command class in the {\ttfamily itcl\+::class} meaning.

\label{config_cfg_optimize_output_for_c}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_optimize_output_for_c}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+C} ]\index{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_FOR\_C@{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_FOR\_C}} Set the {\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+C} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} sources only. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then generate output that is more tailored for \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}. For instance, some of the names that are used will be different. The list of all members will be omitted, etc.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_optimize_output_java}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_optimize_output_java}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+J\+A\+VA} ]\index{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_JAVA@{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_JAVA}} Set the {\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+J\+A\+VA} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of Java or Python sources only. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then generate output that is more tailored for that language. For instance, namespaces will be presented as packages, qualified scopes will look different, etc.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_optimize_for_fortran}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_optimize_for_fortran}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+T\+R\+AN} ]\index{OPTIMIZE\_FOR\_FORTRAN@{OPTIMIZE\_FOR\_FORTRAN}} Set the {\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+T\+R\+AN} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of Fortran sources. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then generate output that is tailored for Fortran.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_optimize_output_vhdl}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_optimize_output_vhdl}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+V\+H\+DL} ]\index{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_VHDL@{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_VHDL}} Set the {\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+V\+H\+DL} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of V\+H\+DL sources. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then generate output that is tailored for V\+H\+DL.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_optimize_output_slice}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_optimize_output_slice}%

\item[{\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+S\+L\+I\+CE} ]\index{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_SLICE@{OPTIMIZE\_OUTPUT\_SLICE}} Set the {\ttfamily O\+P\+T\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+S\+L\+I\+CE} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of Slice sources only. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then generate output that is more tailored for that language. For instance, namespaces will be presented as modules, types will be separated into more groups, etc.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extension_mapping}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extension_mapping}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG} ]\index{EXTENSION\_MAPPING@{EXTENSION\_MAPPING}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} selects the parser to use depending on the extension of the files it parses. With this tag you can assign which parser to use for a given extension. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} has a built-\/in mapping, but you can override or extend it using this tag. The format is {\ttfamily ext=language}, where {\ttfamily ext} is a file extension, and language is one of the parsers supported by doxygen\+: I\+DL, Java, Javascript, Csharp (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}\#), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}, C++, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_d}{D}}, P\+HP, md (Markdown), Objective-\/C, Python, Slice, Fortran (fixed format Fortran\+: Fortran\+Fixed, free formatted Fortran\+: Fortran\+Free, unknown formatted Fortran\+: Fortran. In the later case the parser tries to guess whether the code is fixed or free formatted code, this is the default for Fortran type files), V\+H\+DL, tcl.

For instance to make doxygen treat {\ttfamily .inc} files as Fortran files (default is P\+HP), and {\ttfamily .f} files as \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} (default is Fortran), use\+: {\ttfamily inc=Fortran f=\mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}}.

~\newline
Note\+: For files without extension you can use {\ttfamily no\+\_\+extension} as a placeholder. ~\newline
Note that for custom extensions you also need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_file_patterns}{F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS}} otherwise the files are not read by doxygen.

\label{config_cfg_markdown_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_markdown_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+R\+K\+D\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{MARKDOWN\_SUPPORT@{MARKDOWN\_SUPPORT}} If the {\ttfamily M\+A\+R\+K\+D\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} tag is enabled then doxygen pre-\/processes all comments according to the Markdown format, which allows for more readable documentation. See \href{https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/}{\texttt{ https\+://daringfireball.\+net/projects/markdown/}} for details. The output of markdown processing is further processed by doxygen, so you can mix doxygen, H\+T\+ML, and X\+ML commands with Markdown formatting. Disable only in case of backward compatibilities issues.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_toc_include_headings}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_toc_include_headings}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+O\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+I\+N\+GS} ]\index{TOC\_INCLUDE\_HEADINGS@{TOC\_INCLUDE\_HEADINGS}} When the {\ttfamily T\+O\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+I\+N\+GS} tag is set to a non-\/zero value, all headings up to that level are automatically included in the table of contents, even if they do not have an id attribute. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This feature currently applies only to Markdown headings.
\end{DoxyNote}
Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 99}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 5}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_markdown_support}{M\+A\+R\+K\+D\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_autolink_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_autolink_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+U\+T\+O\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{AUTOLINK\_SUPPORT@{AUTOLINK\_SUPPORT}} When enabled doxygen tries to link words that correspond to documented classes, or namespaces to their corresponding documentation. Such a link can be prevented in individual cases by putting a {\ttfamily \%} sign in front of the word or globally by setting {\ttfamily A\+U\+T\+O\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} to {\ttfamily NO}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_builtin_stl_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_builtin_stl_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily B\+U\+I\+L\+T\+I\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+L\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{BUILTIN\_STL\_SUPPORT@{BUILTIN\_STL\_SUPPORT}} If you use S\+TL classes (i.\+e. {\ttfamily std\+::string}, {\ttfamily std\+::vector}, etc.) but do not want to include (a tag file for) the S\+TL sources as input, then you should set this tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} in order to let doxygen match functions declarations and definitions whose arguments contain S\+TL classes (e.\+g. {\ttfamily func(std\+::string}); versus {\ttfamily func(std\+::string) \{\}}). This also make the inheritance and collaboration diagrams that involve S\+TL classes more complete and accurate.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_cpp_cli_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_cpp_cli_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+P\+P\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{CPP\_CLI\_SUPPORT@{CPP\_CLI\_SUPPORT}} If you use Microsoft\textquotesingle{}s C++/\+C\+LI language, you should set this option to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to enable parsing support.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_sip_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sip_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{SIP\_SUPPORT@{SIP\_SUPPORT}} Set the {\ttfamily S\+I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if your project consists of \href{https://www.riverbankcomputing.com/software/sip/intro}{\texttt{ sip}} sources only. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will parse them like normal C++ but will assume all classes use public instead of private inheritance when no explicit protection keyword is present.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_idl_property_support}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_idl_property_support}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+D\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT} ]\index{IDL\_PROPERTY\_SUPPORT@{IDL\_PROPERTY\_SUPPORT}} For Microsoft\textquotesingle{}s I\+DL there are {\ttfamily propget} and {\ttfamily propput} attributes to indicate getter and setter methods for a property. Setting this option to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} will make doxygen to replace the get and set methods by a property in the documentation. This will only work if the methods are indeed getting or setting a simple type. If this is not the case, or you want to show the methods anyway, you should set this option to {\ttfamily NO}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_distribute_group_doc}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_distribute_group_doc}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+S\+T\+R\+I\+B\+U\+T\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+D\+OC} ]\index{DISTRIBUTE\_GROUP\_DOC@{DISTRIBUTE\_GROUP\_DOC}} If member grouping is used in the documentation and the {\ttfamily D\+I\+S\+T\+R\+I\+B\+U\+T\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+D\+OC} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will reuse the documentation of the first member in the group (if any) for the other members of the group. By default all members of a group must be documented explicitly.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_group_nested_compounds}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_group_nested_compounds}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+S\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+U\+N\+DS} ]\index{GROUP\_NESTED\_COMPOUNDS@{GROUP\_NESTED\_COMPOUNDS}} If one adds a struct or class to a group and this option is enabled, then also any nested class or struct is added to the same group. By default this option is disabled and one has to add nested compounds explicitly via \textbackslash{}ingroup.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_subgrouping}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_subgrouping}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+U\+B\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+I\+NG} ]\index{SUBGROUPING@{SUBGROUPING}} Set the {\ttfamily S\+U\+B\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+I\+NG} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to allow class member groups of the same type (for instance a group of public functions) to be put as a subgroup of that type (e.\+g. under the Public Functions section). Set it to {\ttfamily NO} to prevent subgrouping. Alternatively, this can be done per class using the \textbackslash{}nosubgrouping command.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_inline_grouped_classes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inline_grouped_classes}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+E\+D\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} ]\index{INLINE\_GROUPED\_CLASSES@{INLINE\_GROUPED\_CLASSES}} When the {\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+E\+D\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, classes, structs and unions are shown inside the group in which they are included (e.\+g. using \textbackslash{}ingroup) instead of on a separate page (for H\+T\+ML and Man pages) or section (for $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ and R\+TF). ~\newline
Note that this feature does not work in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_separate_member_pages}{S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES}}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_inline_simple_structs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inline_simple_structs}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+U\+C\+TS} ]\index{INLINE\_SIMPLE\_STRUCTS@{INLINE\_SIMPLE\_STRUCTS}} When the {\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+U\+C\+TS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, structs, classes, and unions with only public data fields or simple typedef fields will be shown inline in the documentation of the scope in which they are defined (i.\+e. file, namespace, or group documentation), provided this scope is documented. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, structs, classes, and unions are shown on a separate page (for H\+T\+ML and Man pages) or section (for $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ and R\+TF).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_typedef_hides_struct}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_typedef_hides_struct}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+Y\+P\+E\+D\+E\+F\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+U\+CT} ]\index{TYPEDEF\_HIDES\_STRUCT@{TYPEDEF\_HIDES\_STRUCT}} When {\ttfamily T\+Y\+P\+E\+D\+E\+F\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+U\+CT} tag is enabled, a typedef of a struct, union, or enum is documented as struct, union, or enum with the name of the typedef. So {\ttfamily typedef struct TypeS \{\} TypeT}, will appear in the documentation as a struct with name {\ttfamily TypeT}. When disabled the typedef will appear as a member of a file, namespace, or class. And the struct will be named {\ttfamily TypeS}. This can typically be useful for \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} code in case the coding convention dictates that all compound types are typedef\textquotesingle{}ed and only the typedef is referenced, never the tag name.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_lookup_cache_size}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_lookup_cache_size}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+O\+O\+K\+U\+P\+\_\+\+C\+A\+C\+H\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE} ]\index{LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE@{LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE}} The size of the symbol lookup cache can be set using {\ttfamily L\+O\+O\+K\+U\+P\+\_\+\+C\+A\+C\+H\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}. This cache is used to resolve symbols given their name and scope. Since this can be an expensive process and often the same symbol appears multiple times in the code, doxygen keeps a cache of pre-\/resolved symbols. If the cache is too small doxygen will become slower. If the cache is too large, memory is wasted. The cache size is given by this formula\+: $2^{(16+\mbox{LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE})}$. The valid range is 0..9, the default is 0, corresponding to a cache size of $2^{16} = 65536$ symbols. At the end of a run doxygen will report the cache usage and suggest the optimal cache size from a speed point of view.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 9}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 0}.


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_build}{}\doxysection{Build related configuration options}\label{config_config_build}
\label{config_cfg_extract_all}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_all}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL} ]\index{EXTRACT\_ALL@{EXTRACT\_ALL}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will assume all entities in documentation are documented, even if no documentation was available. Private class members and static file members will be hidden unless the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_private}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+TE}} respectively \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_static}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+IC}} tags are set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This will also disable the warnings about undocumented members that are normally produced when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_warnings}{W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+GS}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.
\end{DoxyNote}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_private}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_private}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+TE} ]\index{EXTRACT\_PRIVATE@{EXTRACT\_PRIVATE}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+TE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all private members of a class will be included in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_priv_virtual}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_priv_virtual}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+AL} ]\index{EXTRACT\_PRIV\_VIRTUAL@{EXTRACT\_PRIV\_VIRTUAL}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+AL} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, documented private virtual methods of a class will be included in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_package}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_package}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+A\+GE} ]\index{EXTRACT\_PACKAGE@{EXTRACT\_PACKAGE}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+A\+GE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all members with package or internal scope will be included in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_static}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_static}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+IC} ]\index{EXTRACT\_STATIC@{EXTRACT\_STATIC}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+IC} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all static members of a file will be included in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_local_classes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_local_classes}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} ]\index{EXTRACT\_LOCAL\_CLASSES@{EXTRACT\_LOCAL\_CLASSES}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, classes (and structs) defined locally in source files will be included in the documentation. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only classes defined in header files are included. Does not have any effect for Java sources.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_local_methods}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_local_methods}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+DS} ]\index{EXTRACT\_LOCAL\_METHODS@{EXTRACT\_LOCAL\_METHODS}} This flag is only useful for Objective-\/C code. If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, local methods, which are defined in the implementation section but not in the interface are included in the documentation. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only methods in the interface are included.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_extract_anon_nspaces}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extract_anon_nspaces}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+O\+N\+\_\+\+N\+S\+P\+A\+C\+ES} ]\index{EXTRACT\_ANON\_NSPACES@{EXTRACT\_ANON\_NSPACES}} If this flag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the members of anonymous namespaces will be extracted and appear in the documentation as a namespace called \textquotesingle{}anonymous\+\_\+namespace\{file\}\textquotesingle{}, where file will be replaced with the base name of the file that contains the anonymous namespace. By default anonymous namespace are hidden.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_hide_undoc_members}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_undoc_members}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+RS} ]\index{HIDE\_UNDOC\_MEMBERS@{HIDE\_UNDOC\_MEMBERS}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+RS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will hide all undocumented members inside documented classes or files. If set to {\ttfamily NO} these members will be included in the various overviews, but no documentation section is generated. This option has no effect if \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_all}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL}} is enabled.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_hide_undoc_classes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_undoc_classes}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} ]\index{HIDE\_UNDOC\_CLASSES@{HIDE\_UNDOC\_CLASSES}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will hide all undocumented classes that are normally visible in the class hierarchy. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, these classes will be included in the various overviews. This option has no effect if \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_all}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL}} is enabled.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_hide_friend_compounds}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_friend_compounds}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+U\+N\+DS} ]\index{HIDE\_FRIEND\_COMPOUNDS@{HIDE\_FRIEND\_COMPOUNDS}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+U\+N\+DS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will hide all friend (class$\vert$struct$\vert$union) declarations. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, these declarations will be included in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_hide_in_body_docs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_in_body_docs}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+B\+O\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} ]\index{HIDE\_IN\_BODY\_DOCS@{HIDE\_IN\_BODY\_DOCS}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+B\+O\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will hide any documentation blocks found inside the body of a function. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, these blocks will be appended to the function\textquotesingle{}s detailed documentation block.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_internal_docs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_internal_docs}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} ]\index{INTERNAL\_DOCS@{INTERNAL\_DOCS}} The {\ttfamily I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} tag determines if documentation that is typed after a \textbackslash{}internal command is included. If the tag is set to {\ttfamily NO} then the documentation will be excluded. Set it to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to include the internal documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_case_sense_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_case_sense_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{CASE\_SENSE\_NAMES@{CASE\_SENSE\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily C\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily NO} then doxygen will only generate file names in lower-\/case letters. If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, upper-\/case letters are also allowed. This is useful if you have classes or files whose names only differ in case and if your file system supports case sensitive file names. Windows (including Cygwin) ands Mac users are advised to set this option to {\ttfamily NO}.

The default value is\+: system dependent.

\label{config_cfg_hide_scope_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_scope_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{HIDE\_SCOPE\_NAMES@{HIDE\_SCOPE\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily NO} then doxygen will show members with their full class and namespace scopes in the documentation. If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the scope will be hidden.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_hide_compound_reference}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_compound_reference}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+CE} ]\index{HIDE\_COMPOUND\_REFERENCE@{HIDE\_COMPOUND\_REFERENCE}} If the {\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+CE} tag is set to {\ttfamily NO} (default) then doxygen will append additional text to a page\textquotesingle{}s title, such as Class Reference. If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} the compound reference will be hidden.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_show_include_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_show_include_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{SHOW\_INCLUDE\_FILES@{SHOW\_INCLUDE\_FILES}} If the {\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will put a list of the files that are included by a file in the documentation of that file.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_show_grouped_memb_inc}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_show_grouped_memb_inc}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+\_\+\+I\+NC} ]\index{SHOW\_GROUPED\_MEMB\_INC@{SHOW\_GROUPED\_MEMB\_INC}} If the S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+\_\+\+I\+NC tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will add for each grouped member an include statement to the documentation, telling the reader which file to include in order to use the member.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_force_local_includes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_force_local_includes}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+O\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES} ]\index{FORCE\_LOCAL\_INCLUDES@{FORCE\_LOCAL\_INCLUDES}} If the {\ttfamily F\+O\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will list include files with double quotes in the documentation rather than with sharp brackets.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_inline_info}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inline_info}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO} ]\index{INLINE\_INFO@{INLINE\_INFO}} If the {\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then a tag \mbox{[}inline\mbox{]} is inserted in the documentation for inline members.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_sort_member_docs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sort_member_docs}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} ]\index{SORT\_MEMBER\_DOCS@{SORT\_MEMBER\_DOCS}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will sort the (detailed) documentation of file and class members alphabetically by member name. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the members will appear in declaration order.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_sort_brief_docs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sort_brief_docs}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} ]\index{SORT\_BRIEF\_DOCS@{SORT\_BRIEF\_DOCS}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will sort the brief descriptions of file, namespace and class members alphabetically by member name. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the members will appear in declaration order. Note that this will also influence the order of the classes in the class list.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_sort_members_ctors_1st}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sort_members_ctors_1st}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+S\+\_\+\+C\+T\+O\+R\+S\+\_\+1\+ST} ]\index{SORT\_MEMBERS\_CTORS\_1ST@{SORT\_MEMBERS\_CTORS\_1ST}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+S\+\_\+\+C\+T\+O\+R\+S\+\_\+1\+ST} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will sort the (brief and detailed) documentation of class members so that constructors and destructors are listed first. If set to {\ttfamily NO} the constructors will appear in the respective orders defined by \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_sort_brief_docs}{S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_sort_member_docs}{S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS}}. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_sort_brief_docs}{S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+E\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS}} is set to {\ttfamily NO} this option is ignored for sorting brief member documentation. 

If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_sort_member_docs}{S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+O\+CS}} is set to {\ttfamily NO} this option is ignored for sorting detailed member documentation.
\end{DoxyNote}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_sort_group_names}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sort_group_names}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} ]\index{SORT\_GROUP\_NAMES@{SORT\_GROUP\_NAMES}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will sort the hierarchy of group names into alphabetical order. If set to {\ttfamily NO} the group names will appear in their defined order.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_sort_by_scope_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_sort_by_scope_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{SORT\_BY\_SCOPE\_NAME@{SORT\_BY\_SCOPE\_NAME}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the class list will be sorted by fully-\/qualified names, including namespaces. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, the class list will be sorted only by class name, not including the namespace part. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This option is not very useful if \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_hide_scope_names}{H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+ES}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 

This option applies only to the class list, not to the alphabetical list.
\end{DoxyNote}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_strict_proto_matching}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_strict_proto_matching}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+C\+H\+I\+NG} ]\index{STRICT\_PROTO\_MATCHING@{STRICT\_PROTO\_MATCHING}} If the {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+C\+H\+I\+NG} option is enabled and doxygen fails to do proper type resolution of all parameters of a function it will reject a match between the prototype and the implementation of a member function even if there is only one candidate or it is obvious which candidate to choose by doing a simple string match. By disabling {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+C\+H\+I\+NG} doxygen will still accept a match between prototype and implementation in such cases.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_generate_todolist}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_todolist}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+D\+O\+L\+I\+ST} ]\index{GENERATE\_TODOLIST@{GENERATE\_TODOLIST}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+D\+O\+L\+I\+ST} tag can be used to enable ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or disable ({\ttfamily NO}) the todo list. This list is created by putting \textbackslash{}todo commands in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_generate_testlist}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_testlist}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+L\+I\+ST} ]\index{GENERATE\_TESTLIST@{GENERATE\_TESTLIST}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+L\+I\+ST} tag can be used to enable ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or disable ({\ttfamily NO}) the test list. This list is created by putting \textbackslash{}test commands in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_generate_buglist}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_buglist}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+G\+L\+I\+ST} ]\index{GENERATE\_BUGLIST@{GENERATE\_BUGLIST}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+G\+L\+I\+ST} tag can be used to enable ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or disable ({\ttfamily NO}) the bug list. This list is created by putting \textbackslash{}bug commands in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_generate_deprecatedlist}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_deprecatedlist}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+E\+D\+L\+I\+ST} ]\index{GENERATE\_DEPRECATEDLIST@{GENERATE\_DEPRECATEDLIST}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+E\+D\+L\+I\+ST} tag can be used to enable ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or disable ({\ttfamily NO}) the deprecated list. This list is created by putting \textbackslash{}deprecated commands in the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_enabled_sections}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_enabled_sections}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{ENABLED\_SECTIONS@{ENABLED\_SECTIONS}} The {\ttfamily E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+NS} tag can be used to enable conditional documentation sections, marked by \textbackslash{}if $<$section\+\_\+label$>$ ... \textbackslash{}endif and \textbackslash{}cond $<$section\+\_\+label$>$ ... \textbackslash{}endcond blocks.

\label{config_cfg_max_initializer_lines}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_max_initializer_lines}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+E\+R\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+ES} ]\index{MAX\_INITIALIZER\_LINES@{MAX\_INITIALIZER\_LINES}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+E\+R\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+ES} tag determines the maximum number of lines that the initial value of a variable or macro / define can have for it to appear in the documentation. If the initializer consists of more lines than specified here it will be hidden. Use a value of 0 to hide initializers completely. The appearance of the value of individual variables and macros / defines can be controlled using \textbackslash{}showinitializer or \textbackslash{}hideinitializer command in the documentation regardless of this setting.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 10000}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 30}.

\label{config_cfg_show_used_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_show_used_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{SHOW\_USED\_FILES@{SHOW\_USED\_FILES}} Set the {\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag to {\ttfamily NO} to disable the list of files generated at the bottom of the documentation of classes and structs. If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the list will mention the files that were used to generate the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_show_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_show_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{SHOW\_FILES@{SHOW\_FILES}} Set the {\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag to {\ttfamily NO} to disable the generation of the Files page. This will remove the Files entry from the Quick Index and from the Folder Tree View (if specified).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_show_namespaces}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_show_namespaces}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+S\+P\+A\+C\+ES} ]\index{SHOW\_NAMESPACES@{SHOW\_NAMESPACES}} Set the {\ttfamily S\+H\+O\+W\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+S\+P\+A\+C\+ES} tag to {\ttfamily NO} to disable the generation of the Namespaces page. This will remove the Namespaces entry from the Quick Index and from the Folder Tree View (if specified).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_file_version_filter}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_file_version_filter}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} ]\index{FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER@{FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER}} The {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} tag can be used to specify a program or script that doxygen should invoke to get the current version for each file (typically from the version control system). \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will invoke the program by executing (via {\ttfamily popen()}) the command {\ttfamily command input-\/file}, where {\ttfamily command} is the value of the {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} tag, and {\ttfamily input-\/file} is the name of an input file provided by doxygen. Whatever the program writes to standard output is used as the file version.~\newline
 ~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_example}{Example}} of using a shell script as a filter for Unix\+: \begin{DoxyVerb} FILE_VERSION_FILTER = "/bin/sh versionfilter.sh"
\end{DoxyVerb}
 ~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_example}{Example}} shell script for C\+VS\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}#!/bin/sh
cvs status $1 | sed -n 's/^[ \]*Working revision:[ \t]*\([0-9][0-9\.]*\).*/\1/p'
\end{DoxyVerb}
 ~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_example}{Example}} shell script for Subversion\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}#!/bin/sh
svn stat -v $1 | sed -n 's/^[ A-Z?\*|!]\{1,15\}/r/;s/ \{1,15\}/\/r/;s/ .*//p'
\end{DoxyVerb}
 ~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_example}{Example}} filter for Clear\+Case\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}FILE_VERSION_FILTER = "cleartool desc -fmt \%Vn"
\end{DoxyVerb}


\label{config_cfg_layout_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_layout_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+Y\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{LAYOUT\_FILE@{LAYOUT\_FILE}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+Y\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify a layout file which will be parsed by doxygen. The layout file controls the global structure of the generated output files in an output format independent way. To create the layout file that represents doxygen\textquotesingle{}s defaults, run doxygen with the {\ttfamily -\/l} option. You can optionally specify a file name after the option, if omitted {\ttfamily Doxygen\+Layout.\+xml} will be used as the name of the layout file. ~\newline
Note that if you run doxygen from a directory containing a file called {\ttfamily Doxygen\+Layout.\+xml}, doxygen will parse it automatically even if the {\ttfamily L\+A\+Y\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag is left empty.

\label{config_cfg_cite_bib_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_cite_bib_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{CITE\_BIB\_FILES@{CITE\_BIB\_FILES}} The {\ttfamily C\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag can be used to specify one or more {\ttfamily bib} files containing the reference definitions. This must be a list of {\ttfamily .bib} files. The {\ttfamily .bib} extension is automatically appended if omitted. This requires the {\ttfamily bibtex} tool to be installed. See also \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BibTeX}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+Bib\+TeX}} for more info. For $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ the style of the bibliography can be controlled using \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_bib_style}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+LE}}. To use this feature you need {\ttfamily bibtex} and {\ttfamily perl} available in the search path. See also \textbackslash{}cite for info how to create references.


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_messages}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to warning and progress messages}\label{config_config_messages}
\label{config_cfg_quiet}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_quiet}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily Q\+U\+I\+ET} ]\index{QUIET@{QUIET}} The {\ttfamily Q\+U\+I\+ET} tag can be used to turn on/off the messages that are generated to standard output by doxygen. If {\ttfamily Q\+U\+I\+ET} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} this implies that the messages are off.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_warnings}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warnings}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+GS} ]\index{WARNINGS@{WARNINGS}} The {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+GS} tag can be used to turn on/off the warning messages that are generated to standard error ({\ttfamily stderr}) by doxygen. If {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+GS} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} this implies that the warnings are on. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Tip\+:}} Turn warnings on while writing the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_if_undocumented}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_if_undocumented}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+I\+F\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+ED} ]\index{WARN\_IF\_UNDOCUMENTED@{WARN\_IF\_UNDOCUMENTED}} If the {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+I\+F\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+ED} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate warnings for undocumented members. If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_all}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then this flag will automatically be disabled.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_if_doc_error}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_if_doc_error}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+I\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} ]\index{WARN\_IF\_DOC\_ERROR@{WARN\_IF\_DOC\_ERROR}} If the {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+I\+F\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate warnings for potential errors in the documentation, such as not documenting some parameters in a documented function, or documenting parameters that don\textquotesingle{}t exist or using markup commands wrongly.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_no_paramdoc}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_no_paramdoc}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+D\+OC} ]\index{WARN\_NO\_PARAMDOC@{WARN\_NO\_PARAMDOC}} This {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+D\+OC} option can be enabled to get warnings for functions that are documented, but have no documentation for their parameters or return value. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, doxygen will only warn about wrong or incomplete parameter documentation, but not about the absence of documentation. If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extract_all}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+A\+LL}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then this flag will automatically be disabled.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_as_error}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_as_error}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} ]\index{WARN\_AS\_ERROR@{WARN\_AS\_ERROR}} If the {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will immediately stop when a warning is encountered.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_format}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_format}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT} ]\index{WARN\_FORMAT@{WARN\_FORMAT}} The {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT} tag determines the format of the warning messages that doxygen can produce. The string should contain the {\ttfamily \$file}, {\ttfamily \$line}, and {\ttfamily \$text} tags, which will be replaced by the file and line number from which the warning originated and the warning text. Optionally the format may contain {\ttfamily \$version}, which will be replaced by the version of the file (if it could be obtained via \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_file_version_filter}{F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER}})

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily \$file\+:\$line\+: \$text}.

\label{config_cfg_warn_logfile}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_warn_logfile}%

\item[{\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{WARN\_LOGFILE@{WARN\_LOGFILE}} The {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify a file to which warning and error messages should be written. If left blank the output is written to standard error ({\ttfamily stderr}).


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_input}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the input files}\label{config_config_input}
\label{config_cfg_input}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_input}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+UT} ]\index{INPUT@{INPUT}} The {\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify the files and/or directories that contain documented source files. You may enter file names like {\ttfamily myfile.\+cpp} or directories like {\ttfamily /usr/src/myproject}. Separate the files or directories with spaces. See also \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_file_patterns}{F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extension_mapping}{E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG}}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this tag is empty the current directory is searched.
\end{DoxyNote}
\label{config_cfg_input_encoding}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_input_encoding}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG} ]\index{INPUT\_ENCODING@{INPUT\_ENCODING}} This tag can be used to specify the character encoding of the source files that doxygen parses. Internally doxygen uses the U\+T\+F-\/8 encoding. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} uses {\ttfamily libiconv} (or the {\ttfamily iconv} built into {\ttfamily libc}) for the transcoding. See \href{https://www.gnu.org/software/libiconv/}{\texttt{ the libiconv documentation}} for the list of possible encodings.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily U\+T\+F-\/8}.

\label{config_cfg_file_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_file_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{FILE\_PATTERNS@{FILE\_PATTERNS}} If the value of the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} tag contains directories, you can use the {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag to specify one or more wildcard patterns (like {\ttfamily $\ast$.cpp} and {\ttfamily $\ast$.h}) to filter out the source-\/files in the directories.~\newline
 Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extension_mapping}{E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG}} for the extension otherwise the files are not read by doxygen.~\newline
 If left blank the following patterns are tested\+: {\ttfamily $\ast$.c}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.cc}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.cxx}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.cpp}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.c++}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.java}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.ii}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.ixx}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.ipp}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.i++}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.inl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.idl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.ddl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.odl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.h}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.hh}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.hxx}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.hpp}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.h++}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.cs}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.d}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.php}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.php4}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.php5}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.phtml}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.inc}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.m}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.markdown}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.md}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.mm}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.dox} (to be provided as doxygen \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} comment), {\ttfamily $\ast$.doc} (to be provided as doxygen \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} comment), {\ttfamily $\ast$.txt} (to be provided as doxygen \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} comment), {\ttfamily $\ast$.py}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.pyw}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.f90}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.f95}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.f03}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.f08}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.f}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.for}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.tcl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.vhd}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.vhdl}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.ucf}, {\ttfamily $\ast$.qsf} and {\ttfamily $\ast$.ice}.

\label{config_cfg_recursive}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_recursive}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+E\+C\+U\+R\+S\+I\+VE} ]\index{RECURSIVE@{RECURSIVE}} The {\ttfamily R\+E\+C\+U\+R\+S\+I\+VE} tag can be used to specify whether or not subdirectories should be searched for input files as well.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_exclude}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_exclude}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+DE} ]\index{EXCLUDE@{EXCLUDE}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+DE} tag can be used to specify files and/or directories that should be excluded from the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} source files. This way you can easily exclude a subdirectory from a directory tree whose root is specified with the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} tag. ~\newline
Note that relative paths are relative to the directory from which doxygen is run.

\label{config_cfg_exclude_symlinks}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_exclude_symlinks}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+M\+L\+I\+N\+KS} ]\index{EXCLUDE\_SYMLINKS@{EXCLUDE\_SYMLINKS}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+M\+L\+I\+N\+KS} tag can be used to select whether or not files or directories that are symbolic links (a Unix file system feature) are excluded from the input.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_exclude_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_exclude_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{EXCLUDE\_PATTERNS@{EXCLUDE\_PATTERNS}} If the value of the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} tag contains directories, you can use the {\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag to specify one or more wildcard patterns to exclude certain files from those directories. ~\newline
Note that the wildcards are matched against the file with absolute path, so to exclude all test directories for example use the pattern {\ttfamily $\ast$}{\ttfamily /test/}{\ttfamily $\ast$}

\label{config_cfg_exclude_symbols}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_exclude_symbols}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+M\+B\+O\+LS} ]\index{EXCLUDE\_SYMBOLS@{EXCLUDE\_SYMBOLS}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+M\+B\+O\+LS} tag can be used to specify one or more symbol names (namespaces, classes, functions, etc.) that should be excluded from the output. The symbol name can be a fully qualified name, a word, or if the wildcard {\ttfamily $\ast$} is used, a substring. Examples\+: {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_a_namespace}{A\+Namespace}}}, {\ttfamily A\+Class}, {\ttfamily A\+Class\+::\+A\+Namespace}, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_a_namespace}{A\+Namespace}}\+:\+:$\ast$\+Test} ~\newline
Note that the wildcards are matched against the file with absolute path, so to exclude all test directories use the pattern {\ttfamily $\ast$}{\ttfamily /test/}{\ttfamily $\ast$}

\label{config_cfg_example_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_example_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{EXAMPLE\_PATH@{EXAMPLE\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to specify one or more files or directories that contain example code fragments that are included (see the \textbackslash{}include command).

\label{config_cfg_example_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_example_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{EXAMPLE\_PATTERNS@{EXAMPLE\_PATTERNS}} If the value of the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_example_path}{E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}} tag contains directories, you can use the {\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag to specify one or more wildcard pattern (like {\ttfamily $\ast$.cpp} and {\ttfamily $\ast$.h}) to filter out the source-\/files in the directories. If left blank all files are included.

\label{config_cfg_example_recursive}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_example_recursive}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+U\+R\+S\+I\+VE} ]\index{EXAMPLE\_RECURSIVE@{EXAMPLE\_RECURSIVE}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+U\+R\+S\+I\+VE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then subdirectories will be searched for input files to be used with the \textbackslash{}include or \textbackslash{}dontinclude commands irrespective of the value of the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_recursive}{R\+E\+C\+U\+R\+S\+I\+VE}} tag.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_image_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_image_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{IMAGE\_PATH@{IMAGE\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to specify one or more files or directories that contain images that are to be included in the documentation (see the \textbackslash{}image command).

\label{config_cfg_input_filter}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_input_filter}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} ]\index{INPUT\_FILTER@{INPUT\_FILTER}} The {\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} tag can be used to specify a program that doxygen should invoke to filter for each input file. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will invoke the filter program by executing (via {\ttfamily popen()}) the command\+: ~\newline
 {\ttfamily $<$filter$>$ $<$input-\/file$>$} ~\newline
 where {\ttfamily $<$filter$>$} is the value of the {\ttfamily I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER} tag, and {\ttfamily $<$input-\/file$>$} is the name of an input file. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then use the output that the filter program writes to standard output. If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_filter_patterns}{F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS}} is specified, this tag will be ignored. ~\newline
Note that the filter must not add or remove lines; it is applied before the code is scanned, but not when the output code is generated. If lines are added or removed, the anchors will not be placed correctly. ~\newline
Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extension_mapping}{E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG}} for the extension otherwise the files are not properly processed by doxygen.~\newline


\label{config_cfg_filter_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_filter_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{FILTER\_PATTERNS@{FILTER\_PATTERNS}} The {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag can be used to specify filters on a per file pattern basis. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will compare the file name with each pattern and apply the filter if there is a match. The filters are a list of the form\+: pattern=filter (like {\ttfamily $\ast$.cpp=my\+\_\+cpp\+\_\+filter}). See \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input_filter}{I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER}} for further information on how filters are used. If the {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag is empty or if none of the patterns match the file name, \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input_filter}{I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER}} is applied. ~\newline
Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extension_mapping}{E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG}} for the extension otherwise the files are not properly processed by doxygen.~\newline


\label{config_cfg_filter_source_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_filter_source_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{FILTER\_SOURCE\_FILES@{FILTER\_SOURCE\_FILES}} If the {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the input filter (if set using \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input_filter}{I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+ER}}) will also be used to filter the input files that are used for producing the source files to browse (i.\+e. when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_filter_source_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_filter_source_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{FILTER\_SOURCE\_PATTERNS@{FILTER\_SOURCE\_PATTERNS}} The {\ttfamily F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag can be used to specify source filters per file pattern. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} pattern will override the setting for \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_filter_patterns}{F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+RN}} (if any) and it is also possible to disable source filtering for a specific pattern using {\ttfamily $\ast$.ext=} (so without naming a filter).

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_filter_source_files}{F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_use_mdfile_as_mainpage}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_use_mdfile_as_mainpage}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+D\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+P\+A\+GE} ]\index{USE\_MDFILE\_AS\_MAINPAGE@{USE\_MDFILE\_AS\_MAINPAGE}} If the {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+D\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+P\+A\+GE} tag refers to the name of a markdown file that is part of the input, its contents will be placed on the main page ({\ttfamily index.\+html}). This can be useful if you have a project on for instance Git\+Hub and want to reuse the introduction page also for the doxygen output.


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_source_browser}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to source browsing}\label{config_config_source_browser}
\label{config_cfg_source_browser}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_source_browser}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER} ]\index{SOURCE\_BROWSER@{SOURCE\_BROWSER}} If the {\ttfamily S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then a list of source files will be generated. Documented entities will be cross-\/referenced with these sources. ~\newline
Note\+: To get rid of all source code in the generated output, make sure that also \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_verbatim_headers}{V\+E\+R\+B\+A\+T\+I\+M\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+E\+RS}} is set to {\ttfamily NO}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_inline_sources}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_inline_sources}%
