\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} ]\index{INLINE\_SOURCES@{INLINE\_SOURCES}} Setting the {\ttfamily I\+N\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} will include the body of functions, classes and enums directly into the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_strip_code_comments}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_strip_code_comments}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+E\+N\+TS} ]\index{STRIP\_CODE\_COMMENTS@{STRIP\_CODE\_COMMENTS}} Setting the {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+E\+N\+TS} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} will instruct doxygen to hide any special comment blocks from generated source code fragments. Normal \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}, C++ and Fortran comments will always remain visible.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_referenced_by_relation}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_referenced_by_relation}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+D\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} ]\index{REFERENCED\_BY\_RELATION@{REFERENCED\_BY\_RELATION}} If the {\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+D\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then for each documented entity all documented functions referencing it will be listed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_references_relation}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_references_relation}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} ]\index{REFERENCES\_RELATION@{REFERENCES\_RELATION}} If the {\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then for each documented function all documented entities called/used by that function will be listed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_references_link_source}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_references_link_source}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE} ]\index{REFERENCES\_LINK\_SOURCE@{REFERENCES\_LINK\_SOURCE}} If the {\ttfamily R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the hyperlinks from functions in \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_references_relation}{R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_referenced_by_relation}{R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+C\+E\+D\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON}} lists will link to the source code. Otherwise they will link to the documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_source_tooltips}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_source_tooltips}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+L\+T\+I\+PS} ]\index{SOURCE\_TOOLTIPS@{SOURCE\_TOOLTIPS}} If S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+L\+T\+I\+PS is enabled (the default) then hovering a hyperlink in the source code will show a tooltip with additional information such as prototype, brief description and links to the definition and documentation. Since this will make the H\+T\+ML file larger and loading of large files a bit slower, you can opt to disable this feature.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_use_htags}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_use_htags}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+A\+GS} ]\index{USE\_HTAGS@{USE\_HTAGS}} If the {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+A\+GS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the references to source code will point to the H\+T\+ML generated by the {\ttfamily htags(1)} tool instead of doxygen built-\/in source browser. The {\ttfamily htags} tool is part of G\+NU\textquotesingle{}s global source tagging system (see \href{https://www.gnu.org/software/global/global.html}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+gnu.\+org/software/global/global.\+html}}). You will need version 4.\+8.\+6 or higher. ~\newline
 To use it do the following\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Install the latest version of {\ttfamily global} 
\item Enable \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}} and {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+A\+GS} in the configuration file
\item Make sure the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} points to the root of the source tree
\item Run {\ttfamily doxygen} as normal ~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will invoke {\ttfamily htags} (and that will in turn invoke {\ttfamily gtags}), so these tools must be available from the command line (i.\+e. in the search path). ~\newline
 The result\+: instead of the source browser generated by doxygen, the links to source code will now point to the output of {\ttfamily htags}.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_verbatim_headers}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_verbatim_headers}%

\item[{\ttfamily V\+E\+R\+B\+A\+T\+I\+M\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+E\+RS} ]\index{VERBATIM\_HEADERS@{VERBATIM\_HEADERS}} If the {\ttfamily V\+E\+R\+B\+A\+T\+I\+M\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+E\+RS} tag is set the {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a verbatim copy of the header file for each class for which an include is specified. Set to {\ttfamily NO} to disable this. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Section \textbackslash{}class.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_clang_assisted_parsing}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_clang_assisted_parsing}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+N\+G\+\_\+\+A\+S\+S\+I\+S\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+S\+I\+NG} ]\index{CLANG\_ASSISTED\_PARSING@{CLANG\_ASSISTED\_PARSING}} If the {\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+N\+G\+\_\+\+A\+S\+S\+I\+S\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+S\+I\+NG} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will use the \href{http://clang.llvm.org/}{\texttt{ clang parser}} for more accurate parsing at the cost of reduced performance. This can be particularly helpful with template rich C++ code for which doxygen\textquotesingle{}s built-\/in parser lacks the necessary type information.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The availability of this option depends on whether or not doxygen was generated with the {\ttfamily -\/Duse\+\_\+libclang=ON} option for C\+Make.
\end{DoxyNote}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_clang_options}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_clang_options}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{CLANG\_OPTIONS@{CLANG\_OPTIONS}} If clang assisted parsing is enabled you can provide the compiler with command line options that you would normally use when invoking the compiler. Note that the include paths will already be set by doxygen for the files and directories specified with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_input}{I\+N\+P\+UT}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_include_path}{I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_clang_assisted_parsing}{C\+L\+A\+N\+G\+\_\+\+A\+S\+S\+I\+S\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_clang_database_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_clang_database_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+N\+G\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{CLANG\_DATABASE\_PATH@{CLANG\_DATABASE\_PATH}} If clang assisted parsing is enabled you can provide the clang parser with the path to the \href{http://clang.llvm.org/docs/HowToSetupToolingForLLVM.html}{\texttt{ compilation database}} used when the files were built. This is equivalent to specifying the \char`\"{}-\/p\char`\"{} option to a clang tool, such as clang-\/check. These options will then be passed to the parser.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The availability of this option depends on whether or not doxygen was generated with the {\ttfamily -\/Duse\+\_\+libclang=ON} option for C\+Make.
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_index}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the alphabetical class index}\label{config_config_index}
\label{config_cfg_alphabetical_index}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_alphabetical_index}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+B\+E\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} ]\index{ALPHABETICAL\_INDEX@{ALPHABETICAL\_INDEX}} If the {\ttfamily A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+B\+E\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, an alphabetical index of all compounds will be generated. Enable this if the project contains a lot of classes, structs, unions or interfaces.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_cols_in_alpha_index}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_cols_in_alpha_index}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} ]\index{COLS\_IN\_ALPHA\_INDEX@{COLS\_IN\_ALPHA\_INDEX}} The {\ttfamily C\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} tag can be used to specify the number of columns in which the alphabetical index list will be split.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 1}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 20}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 5}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_alphabetical_index}{A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+B\+E\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_ignore_prefix}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_ignore_prefix}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+F\+IX} ]\index{IGNORE\_PREFIX@{IGNORE\_PREFIX}} In case all classes in a project start with a common prefix, all classes will be put under the same header in the alphabetical index. The {\ttfamily I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+F\+IX} tag can be used to specify a prefix (or a list of prefixes) that should be ignored while generating the index headers.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_alphabetical_index}{A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+B\+E\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_html}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the H\+T\+M\+L output}\label{config_config_html}
\label{config_cfg_generate_html}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_html}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML} ]\index{GENERATE\_HTML@{GENERATE\_HTML}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate H\+T\+ML output

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_html_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{HTML\_OUTPUT@{HTML\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the H\+T\+ML docs will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily html}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_file_extension}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_file_extension}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} ]\index{HTML\_FILE\_EXTENSION@{HTML\_FILE\_EXTENSION}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} tag can be used to specify the file extension for each generated H\+T\+ML page (for example\+: {\ttfamily .htm, .php, .asp}).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily .html}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_header}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_header}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} ]\index{HTML\_HEADER@{HTML\_HEADER}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined H\+T\+ML header file for each generated H\+T\+ML page. If the tag is left blank doxygen will generate a standard header. ~\newline
 To get valid H\+T\+ML the header file that includes any scripts and style sheets that doxygen needs, which is dependent on the configuration options used (e.\+g. the setting \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_treeview}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}}). It is highly recommended to start with a default header using \begin{DoxyVerb}doxygen -w html new_header.html new_footer.html new_stylesheet.css YourConfigFile
\end{DoxyVerb}
 and then modify the file {\ttfamily new\+\_\+header.\+html}.

See also section \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage}{Doxygen usage}} for information on how to generate the default header that doxygen normally uses.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The header is subject to change so you typically have to regenerate the default header when upgrading to a newer version of doxygen. The following markers have a special meaning inside the header and footer\+: 
\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily \$title}]will be replaced with the title of the page. 
\item[{\ttfamily \$datetime}]will be replaced with current the date and time. 
\item[{\ttfamily \$date}]will be replaced with the current date. 
\item[{\ttfamily \$year}]will be replaces with the current year. 
\item[{\ttfamily \$doxygenversion}]will be replaced with the version of doxygen 
\item[{\ttfamily \$projectname}]will be replaced with the name of the project (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_name}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}}) 
\item[{\ttfamily \$projectnumber}]will be replaced with the project number (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_number}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER}}) 
\item[{\ttfamily \$projectbrief}]will be replaced with the project brief description (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_brief}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF}}) 
\item[{\ttfamily \$projectlogo}]will be replaced with the project logo (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_logo}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO}}) 
\item[{\ttfamily \$treeview}]will be replaced with links to the javascript and style sheets needed for the navigation tree (or an empty string when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_treeview}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}} is disabled). 
\item[{\ttfamily \$search}]will be replaced with a links to the javascript and style sheets needed for the search engine (or an empty string when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is disabled). 
\item[{\ttfamily \$mathjax}]will be replaced with a links to the javascript and style sheets needed for the Math\+Jax feature (or an empty string when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_mathjax}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX}} is disabled). 
\item[{\ttfamily \$relpath$^\wedge$}]If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_create_subdirs}{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+D\+I\+RS}} is enabled, the command {\ttfamily \$relpath$^\wedge$} can be used to produce a relative path to the root of the H\+T\+ML output directory, e.\+g. use {\ttfamily \$relpath$^\wedge$doxygen.css}, to refer to the standard style sheet. 
\end{DoxyDescription}
\end{DoxyNote}
To cope with differences in the layout of the header and footer that depend on configuration settings, the header can also contain special blocks that will be copied to the output or skipped depending on the configuration. Such blocks have the following form\+: \begin{DoxyVerb} <!--BEGIN BLOCKNAME-->
 Some context copied when condition BLOCKNAME holds
 <!--END BLOCKNAME-->
 <!--BEGIN !BLOCKNAME-->
 Some context copied when condition BLOCKNAME does not hold
 <!--END !BLOCKNAME-->
\end{DoxyVerb}
 The following block names are supported\+: 
\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}]Content within this block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_disable_index}{D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}} option is enabled (so when the index is disabled). 
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}]Content within this block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_treeview}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}} option is enabled. 
\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}]Content within this block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} option is enabled. 
\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}]Content within the block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_name}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}} option is not empty. 
\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER}]Content within the block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_number}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER}} option is not empty. 
\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF}]Content within the block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_brief}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF}} option is not empty. 
\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO}]Content within the block is copied to the output when the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_logo}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO}} option is not empty. 
\item[{\ttfamily T\+I\+T\+L\+E\+A\+R\+EA}]Content within this block is copied to the output when a title is visible at the top of each page. This is the case if either \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_name}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_brief}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+B\+R\+I\+EF}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_logo}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+GO}} is filled in or if both \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_disable_index}{D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} are enabled. 
\end{DoxyDescription}

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_footer}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_footer}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+O\+T\+ER} ]\index{HTML\_FOOTER@{HTML\_FOOTER}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+O\+T\+ER} tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined H\+T\+ML footer for each generated H\+T\+ML page. If the tag is left blank doxygen will generate a standard footer.

See \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_header}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER}} for more information on how to generate a default footer and what special commands can be used inside the footer.

See also section \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage}{Doxygen usage}} for information on how to generate the default footer that doxygen normally uses.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_stylesheet}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_stylesheet}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} ]\index{HTML\_STYLESHEET@{HTML\_STYLESHEET}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined cascading style sheet that is used by each H\+T\+ML page. It can be used to fine-\/tune the look of the H\+T\+ML output. If left blank doxygen will generate a default style sheet.

See also section \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage}{Doxygen usage}} for information on how to generate the style sheet that doxygen normally uses.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
It is recommended to use \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_extra_stylesheet}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET}} instead of this tag, as it is more robust and this tag ({\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET}) will in the future become obsolete.
\end{DoxyNote}
This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_extra_stylesheet}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_extra_stylesheet}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} ]\index{HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET@{HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} tag can be used to specify additional user-\/defined cascading style sheets that are included after the standard style sheets created by doxygen. Using this option one can overrule certain style aspects. This is preferred over using \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_stylesheet}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET}} since it does not replace the standard style sheet and is therefore more robust against future updates. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will copy the style sheet files to the output directory. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The order of the extra style sheet files is of importance (e.\+g. the last style sheet in the list overrules the setting of the previous ones in the list). Here is an example style sheet that gives the contents area a fixed width\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}body {
        background-color: #CCC;
        color: black;
        margin: 0;
}

div.contents {
        margin-bottom: 10px;
        padding: 12px;
        margin-left: auto;
        margin-right: auto;
        width: 960px;
        background-color: white;
        border-radius: 8px;
}

#titlearea {
        background-color: white;
}

hr.footer {
        display: none;
}

.footer {
        background-color: #AAA;
}
\end{DoxyVerb}

\end{DoxyNote}
This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_extra_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_extra_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{HTML\_EXTRA\_FILES@{HTML\_EXTRA\_FILES}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag can be used to specify one or more extra images or other source files which should be copied to the H\+T\+ML output directory. Note that these files will be copied to the base H\+T\+ML output directory. Use the {\ttfamily \$relpath$^\wedge$} marker in the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_header}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER}} and/or \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_footer}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+O\+T\+ER}} files to load these files. In the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_stylesheet}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET}} file, use the file name only. Also note that the files will be copied as-\/is; there are no commands or markers available.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_hue}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_hue}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+UE} ]\index{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_HUE@{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_HUE}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+UE} tag controls the color of the H\+T\+ML output. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will adjust the colors in the style sheet and background images according to this color. Hue is specified as an angle on a colorwheel, see \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hue}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+Hue}} for more information. For instance the value 0 represents red, 60 is yellow, 120 is green, 180 is cyan, 240 is blue, 300 purple, and 360 is red again.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 359}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 220}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_sat}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_sat}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+AT} ]\index{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_SAT@{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_SAT}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+AT} tag controls the purity (or saturation) of the colors in the H\+T\+ML output. For a value of 0 the output will use grayscales only. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} value of 255 will produce the most vivid colors.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 255}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 100}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_gamma}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_colorstyle_gamma}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+MA} ]\index{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_GAMMA@{HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_GAMMA}} The {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+MA} tag controls the gamma correction applied to the luminance component of the colors in the H\+T\+ML output. Values below 100 gradually make the output lighter, whereas values above 100 make the output darker. The value divided by 100 is the actual gamma applied, so 80 represents a gamma of 0.\+8, The value 220 represents a gamma of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace2_1_12}{2.\+2}}, and 100 does not change the gamma.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 40}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 240}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 80}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_timestamp}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_timestamp}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+MP} ]\index{HTML\_TIMESTAMP@{HTML\_TIMESTAMP}} If the {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+MP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the footer of each generated H\+T\+ML page will contain the date and time when the page was generated. Setting this to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} can help to show when doxygen was last run and thus if the documentation is up to date.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_dynamic_menus}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_dynamic_menus}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+I\+C\+\_\+\+M\+E\+N\+US} ]\index{HTML\_DYNAMIC\_MENUS@{HTML\_DYNAMIC\_MENUS}} If the {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+I\+C\+\_\+\+M\+E\+N\+US} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the generated H\+T\+ML documentation will contain a main index with vertical navigation menus that are dynamically created via Javascript. If disabled, the navigation index will consists of multiple levels of tabs that are statically embedded in every H\+T\+ML page. Disable this option to support browsers that do not have Javascript, like the Qt help browser.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_dynamic_sections}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_dynamic_sections}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{HTML\_DYNAMIC\_SECTIONS@{HTML\_DYNAMIC\_SECTIONS}} If the {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+NS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the generated H\+T\+ML documentation will contain sections that can be hidden and shown after the page has loaded.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_html_index_num_entries}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_html_index_num_entries}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+I\+ES} ]\index{HTML\_INDEX\_NUM\_ENTRIES@{HTML\_INDEX\_NUM\_ENTRIES}} With {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+I\+ES} one can control the preferred number of entries shown in the various tree structured indices initially; the user can expand and collapse entries dynamically later on. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will expand the tree to such a level that at most the specified number of entries are visible (unless a fully collapsed tree already exceeds this amount). So setting the number of entries 1 will produce a full collapsed tree by default. 0 is a special value representing an infinite number of entries and will result in a full expanded tree by default.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 9999}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 100}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_docset}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_docset}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET} ]\index{GENERATE\_DOCSET@{GENERATE\_DOCSET}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, additional index files will be generated that can be used as input for \href{https://developer.apple.com/xcode/}{\texttt{ Apple\textquotesingle{}s Xcode 3 integrated development environment}}, introduced with O\+SX 10.\+5 (Leopard). To create a documentation set, doxygen will generate a Makefile in the H\+T\+ML output directory. Running {\ttfamily make} will produce the docset in that directory and running {\ttfamily make install} will install the docset in {\ttfamily $\sim$/\+Library/\+Developer/\+Shared/\+Documentation/\+Doc\+Sets} so that Xcode will find it at startup. See \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/featuredarticles/DoxygenXcode/_index.html}{\texttt{ https\+://developer.\+apple.\+com/library/archive/featuredarticles/\+Doxygen\+Xcode/\+\_\+index.\+html}} for more information.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_docset_feedname}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docset_feedname}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+E\+E\+D\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{DOCSET\_FEEDNAME@{DOCSET\_FEEDNAME}} This tag determines the name of the docset feed. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} documentation feed provides an umbrella under which multiple documentation sets from a single provider (such as a company or product suite) can be grouped.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} generated docs}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docset}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_docset_bundle_id}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docset_bundle_id}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+B\+U\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+ID} ]\index{DOCSET\_BUNDLE\_ID@{DOCSET\_BUNDLE\_ID}} This tag specifies a string that should uniquely identify the documentation set bundle. This should be a reverse domain-\/name style string, e.\+g. {\ttfamily com.\+mycompany.\+My\+Doc\+Set}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will append {\ttfamily .docset} to the name.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily org.\+doxygen.\+Project}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docset}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_docset_publisher_id}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docset_publisher_id}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID} ]\index{DOCSET\_PUBLISHER\_ID@{DOCSET\_PUBLISHER\_ID}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID} tag specifies a string that should uniquely identify the documentation publisher. This should be a reverse domain-\/name style string, e.\+g. {\ttfamily com.\+mycompany.\+My\+Doc\+Set.\+documentation}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily org.\+doxygen.\+Publisher}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docset}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_docset_publisher_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docset_publisher_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{DOCSET\_PUBLISHER\_NAME@{DOCSET\_PUBLISHER\_NAME}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag identifies the documentation publisher.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Publisher}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docset}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP} ]\index{GENERATE\_HTMLHELP@{GENERATE\_HTMLHELP}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen generates three additional H\+T\+ML index files\+: {\ttfamily index.\+hhp}, {\ttfamily index.\+hhc}, and {\ttfamily index.\+hhk}. The {\ttfamily index.\+hhp} is a project file that can be read by \href{https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=21138}{\texttt{ Microsoft\textquotesingle{}s H\+T\+ML Help Workshop}} on Windows. ~\newline
 The H\+T\+ML Help Workshop contains a compiler that can convert all H\+T\+ML output generated by doxygen into a single compiled H\+T\+ML file ({\ttfamily .chm}). Compiled H\+T\+ML files are now used as the Windows 98 help format, and will replace the old Windows help format ({\ttfamily .hlp}) on all Windows platforms in the future. Compressed H\+T\+ML files also contain an index, a table of contents, and you can search for words in the documentation. The H\+T\+ML workshop also contains a viewer for compressed H\+T\+ML files.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_chm_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_chm_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+H\+M\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{CHM\_FILE@{CHM\_FILE}} The {\ttfamily C\+H\+M\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify the file name of the resulting {\ttfamily .chm} file. You can add a path in front of the file if the result should not be written to the html output directory.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_hhc_location}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hhc_location}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+H\+C\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} ]\index{HHC\_LOCATION@{HHC\_LOCATION}} The {\ttfamily H\+H\+C\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} tag can be used to specify the location (absolute path including file name) of the H\+T\+ML help compiler ({\ttfamily hhc.\+exe}). If non-\/empty, doxygen will try to run the H\+T\+ML help compiler on the generated {\ttfamily index.\+hhp}.

The file has to be specified with full path.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_chi}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_chi}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+HI} ]\index{GENERATE\_CHI@{GENERATE\_CHI}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+HI} flag controls if a separate {\ttfamily .chi} index file is generated ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or that it should be included in the master {\ttfamily .chm} file ({\ttfamily NO}).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_chm_index_encoding}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_chm_index_encoding}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+H\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG} ]\index{CHM\_INDEX\_ENCODING@{CHM\_INDEX\_ENCODING}} The {\ttfamily C\+H\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG} is used to encode \mbox{\hyperlink{class_html_help}{Html\+Help}} index ({\ttfamily hhk}), content ({\ttfamily hhc}) and project file content.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_binary_toc}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_binary_toc}%

\item[{\ttfamily B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+OC} ]\index{BINARY\_TOC@{BINARY\_TOC}} The {\ttfamily B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+OC} flag controls whether a binary table of contents is generated ({\ttfamily Y\+ES}) or a normal table of contents ({\ttfamily NO}) in the {\ttfamily .chm} file. Furthermore it enables the {\ttfamily Previous} and {\ttfamily Next} buttons.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_toc_expand}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_toc_expand}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+O\+C\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+ND} ]\index{TOC\_EXPAND@{TOC\_EXPAND}} The {\ttfamily T\+O\+C\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+ND} flag can be set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to add extra items for group members to the table of contents of the H\+T\+ML help documentation and to the tree view.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_qhp}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_qhp}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP} ]\index{GENERATE\_QHP@{GENERATE\_QHP}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} and both \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_qhp_namespace}{Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+S\+P\+A\+CE}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_qhp_virtual_folder}{Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+L\+D\+ER}} are set, an additional index file will be generated that can be used as input for Qt\textquotesingle{}s qhelpgenerator to generate a Qt Compressed Help ({\ttfamily .qch}) of the generated H\+T\+ML documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qch_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qch_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{QCH\_FILE@{QCH\_FILE}} If the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_qhg_location}{Q\+H\+G\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON}} tag is specified, the {\ttfamily Q\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify the file name of the resulting {\ttfamily .qch} file. The path specified is relative to the H\+T\+ML output folder.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhp_namespace}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhp_namespace}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+S\+P\+A\+CE} ]\index{QHP\_NAMESPACE@{QHP\_NAMESPACE}} The {\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+S\+P\+A\+CE} tag specifies the namespace to use when generating Qt Help Project output. For more information please see \href{https://doc.qt.io/archives/qt-4.8/qthelpproject.html\#namespace}{\texttt{ Qt Help Project / Namespace}}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily org.\+doxygen.\+Project}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhp_virtual_folder}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhp_virtual_folder}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+L\+D\+ER} ]\index{QHP\_VIRTUAL\_FOLDER@{QHP\_VIRTUAL\_FOLDER}} The {\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+L\+D\+ER} tag specifies the namespace to use when generating Qt Help Project output. For more information please see \href{https://doc.qt.io/archives/qt-4.8/qthelpproject.html\#virtual-folders}{\texttt{ Qt Help Project / Virtual Folders}}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily doc}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhp_cust_filter_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhp_cust_filter_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{QHP\_CUST\_FILTER\_NAME@{QHP\_CUST\_FILTER\_NAME}} If the {\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag is set, it specifies the name of a custom filter to add. For more information please see \href{https://doc.qt.io/archives/qt-4.8/qthelpproject.html\#custom-filters}{\texttt{ Qt Help Project / Custom Filters}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhp_cust_filter_attrs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhp_cust_filter_attrs}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+RS} ]\index{QHP\_CUST\_FILTER\_ATTRS@{QHP\_CUST\_FILTER\_ATTRS}} The {\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+RS} tag specifies the list of the attributes of the custom filter to add. For more information please see \href{https://doc.qt.io/archives/qt-4.8/qthelpproject.html\#custom-filters}{\texttt{ Qt Help Project / Custom Filters}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhp_sect_filter_attrs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhp_sect_filter_attrs}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+RS} ]\index{QHP\_SECT\_FILTER\_ATTRS@{QHP\_SECT\_FILTER\_ATTRS}} The {\ttfamily Q\+H\+P\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+RS} tag specifies the list of the attributes this project\textquotesingle{}s filter section matches. \href{https://doc.qt.io/archives/qt-4.8/qthelpproject.html\#filter-attributes}{\texttt{ Qt Help Project / Filter Attributes}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_qhg_location}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_qhg_location}%

\item[{\ttfamily Q\+H\+G\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} ]\index{QHG\_LOCATION@{QHG\_LOCATION}} The {\ttfamily Q\+H\+G\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} tag can be used to specify the location of Qt\textquotesingle{}s qhelpgenerator. If non-\/empty doxygen will try to run qhelpgenerator on the generated {\ttfamily .qhp} file.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_eclipsehelp}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_eclipsehelp}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+E\+C\+L\+I\+P\+S\+E\+H\+E\+LP} ]\index{GENERATE\_ECLIPSEHELP@{GENERATE\_ECLIPSEHELP}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+E\+C\+L\+I\+P\+S\+E\+H\+E\+LP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, additional index files will be generated, together with the H\+T\+ML files, they form an {\ttfamily Eclipse} help plugin.

To install this plugin and make it available under the help contents menu in {\ttfamily Eclipse}, the contents of the directory containing the H\+T\+ML and X\+ML files needs to be copied into the plugins directory of eclipse. The name of the directory within the plugins directory should be the same as the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_eclipse_doc_id}{E\+C\+L\+I\+P\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+ID}} value.

After copying {\ttfamily Eclipse} needs to be restarted before the help appears.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_eclipse_doc_id}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_eclipse_doc_id}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+C\+L\+I\+P\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+ID} ]\index{ECLIPSE\_DOC\_ID@{ECLIPSE\_DOC\_ID}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} unique identifier for the {\ttfamily Eclipse} help plugin. When installing the plugin the directory name containing the H\+T\+ML and X\+ML files should also have this name. Each documentation set should have its own identifier.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily org.\+doxygen.\+Project}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_eclipsehelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+E\+C\+L\+I\+P\+S\+E\+H\+E\+LP}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_disable_index}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_disable_index}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} ]\index{DISABLE\_INDEX@{DISABLE\_INDEX}} If you want full control over the layout of the generated H\+T\+ML pages it might be necessary to disable the index and replace it with your own. The {\ttfamily D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX} tag can be used to turn on/off the condensed index (tabs) at top of each H\+T\+ML page. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} value of {\ttfamily NO} enables the index and the value {\ttfamily Y\+ES} disables it. Since the tabs in the index contain the same information as the navigation tree, you can set this option to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} if you also set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_treeview}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}} to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_treeview}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_treeview}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW} ]\index{GENERATE\_TREEVIEW@{GENERATE\_TREEVIEW}} The {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW} tag is used to specify whether a tree-\/like index structure should be generated to display hierarchical information. If the tag value is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, a side panel will be generated containing a tree-\/like index structure (just like the one that is generated for H\+T\+ML Help). For this to work a browser that supports Java\+Script, D\+H\+T\+ML, C\+SS and frames is required (i.\+e. any modern browser). Windows users are probably better off using the H\+T\+ML help feature.

Via custom style sheets (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_extra_stylesheet}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET}}) one can further \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage_doxygen_finetune}{fine-\/tune}} the look of the index. As an example, the default style sheet generated by doxygen has an example that shows how to put an image at the root of the tree instead of the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_project_name}{P\+R\+O\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}}.

Since the tree basically has the same information as the tab index, you could consider setting \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_disable_index}{D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+EX}} to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} when enabling this option.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_enum_values_per_line}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_enum_values_per_line}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+L\+I\+NE} ]\index{ENUM\_VALUES\_PER\_LINE@{ENUM\_VALUES\_PER\_LINE}} The {\ttfamily E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+L\+I\+NE} tag can be used to set the number of enum values that doxygen will group on one line in the generated H\+T\+ML documentation. ~\newline
Note that a value of 0 will completely suppress the enum values from appearing in the overview section.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 20}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 4}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_treeview_width}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_treeview_width}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+E\+W\+\_\+\+W\+I\+D\+TH} ]\index{TREEVIEW\_WIDTH@{TREEVIEW\_WIDTH}} If the treeview is enabled (see \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_treeview}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+V\+I\+EW}}) then this tag can be used to set the initial width (in pixels) of the frame in which the tree is shown.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 1500}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 250}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_ext_links_in_window}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_ext_links_in_window}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+OW} ]\index{EXT\_LINKS\_IN\_WINDOW@{EXT\_LINKS\_IN\_WINDOW}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+OW} option is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will open links to external symbols imported via tag files in a separate window.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_formula_fontsize}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_formula_fontsize}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+O\+R\+M\+U\+L\+A\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+S\+I\+ZE} ]\index{FORMULA\_FONTSIZE@{FORMULA\_FONTSIZE}} Use this tag to change the font size of $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ formulas included as images in the H\+T\+ML documentation. When you change the font size after a successful doxygen run you need to manually remove any {\ttfamily form\+\_\+$\ast$.png} images from the H\+T\+ML output directory to force them to be regenerated.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 8}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 50}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 10}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_formula_transparent}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_formula_transparent}%

\item[{\ttfamily F\+O\+R\+M\+U\+L\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+A\+R\+E\+NT} ]\index{FORMULA\_TRANSPARENT@{FORMULA\_TRANSPARENT}} Use the {\ttfamily F\+O\+R\+M\+U\+L\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+A\+R\+E\+NT} tag to determine whether or not the images generated for formulas are transparent P\+N\+Gs. Transparent P\+N\+Gs are not supported properly for IE 6.\+0, but are supported on all modern browsers. ~\newline
Note that when changing this option you need to delete any {\ttfamily form\+\_\+$\ast$.png} files in the H\+T\+ML output directory before the changes have effect.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_use_mathjax}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_use_mathjax}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX} ]\index{USE\_MATHJAX@{USE\_MATHJAX}} Enable the {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX} option to render $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ formulas using Math\+Jax (see \href{https://www.mathjax.org}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+mathjax.\+org}}) which uses client side Javascript for the rendering instead of using pre-\/rendered bitmaps. Use this if you do not have $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ installed or if you want to formulas look prettier in the H\+T\+ML output. When enabled you may also need to install Math\+Jax separately and configure the path to it using the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_mathjax_relpath}{M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+P\+A\+TH}} option.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_mathjax_format}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_mathjax_format}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT} ]\index{MATHJAX\_FORMAT@{MATHJAX\_FORMAT}} When Math\+Jax is enabled you can set the default output format to be used for the Math\+Jax output. See \href{http://docs.mathjax.org/en/latest/output.html}{\texttt{ the Math\+Jax site}} for more details.

Possible values are\+: {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L-\/\+C\+SS} (which is slower, but has the best compatibility), {\ttfamily Native\+M\+ML} (i.\+e. Math\+ML) and {\ttfamily S\+VG}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily H\+T\+M\+L-\/\+C\+SS}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_mathjax}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_mathjax_relpath}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_mathjax_relpath}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{MATHJAX\_RELPATH@{MATHJAX\_RELPATH}} When Math\+Jax is enabled you need to specify the location relative to the H\+T\+ML output directory using the {\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+P\+A\+TH} option. The destination directory should contain the {\ttfamily Math\+Jax.\+js} script. For instance, if the {\ttfamily mathjax} directory is located at the same level as the H\+T\+ML output directory, then {\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+P\+A\+TH} should be {\ttfamily ../mathjax}. The default value points to the Math\+Jax Content Delivery Network so you can quickly see the result without installing Math\+Jax. However, it is strongly recommended to install a local copy of Math\+Jax from \href{https://www.mathjax.org}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+mathjax.\+org}} before deployment.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily \href{https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/mathjax/2.7.5/}{\texttt{ https\+://cdnjs.\+cloudflare.\+com/ajax/libs/mathjax/2.\+7.\+5/}}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_mathjax}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_mathjax_extensions}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_mathjax_extensions}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS@{MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS} tag can be used to specify one or more Math\+Jax extension names that should be enabled during Math\+Jax rendering. For example \begin{DoxyVerb}MATHJAX_EXTENSIONS     = TeX/AMSmath TeX/AMSsymbols
\end{DoxyVerb}


This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_mathjax}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_mathjax_codefile}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_mathjax_codefile}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{MATHJAX\_CODEFILE@{MATHJAX\_CODEFILE}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+A\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify a file with javascript pieces of code that will be used on startup of the Math\+Jax code. See \href{http://docs.mathjax.org/en/latest/output.html}{\texttt{ the Math\+Jax site}} for more details. As an example to disable the \char`\"{}\+Math Renderer\char`\"{} menu item in the \char`\"{}\+Math
 Settings\char`\"{} menu of Math\+Jax\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}MATHJAX_CODEFILE = disableRenderer.js
\end{DoxyVerb}
 with in the file {\ttfamily disable\+Renderer.\+js}\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}  MathJax.Hub.Config({
   menuSettings: {
    showRenderer: false,
   }
  });
\end{DoxyVerb}


This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_mathjax}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+H\+J\+AX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_searchengine}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_searchengine}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE} ]\index{SEARCHENGINE@{SEARCHENGINE}} When the {\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE} tag is enabled doxygen will generate a search box for the H\+T\+ML output. The underlying search engine uses javascript and D\+H\+T\+ML and should work on any modern browser. Note that when using H\+T\+ML help (\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_htmlhelp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+M\+L\+H\+E\+LP}}), Qt help (\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_qhp}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+Q\+HP}}), or docsets (\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docset}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+S\+ET}}) there is already a search function so this one should typically be disabled. For large projects the javascript based search engine can be slow, then enabling \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_server_based_search}{S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} may provide a better solution.

It is possible to search using the keyboard; to jump to the search box use {\ttfamily $<$access key$>$ + \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_s}{S}}} (what the {\ttfamily $<$access key$>$} is depends on the OS and browser, but it is typically {\ttfamily $<$C\+T\+RL$>$}, {\ttfamily $<$A\+LT$>$}/{\ttfamily $<$option$>$}, or both). Inside the search box use the {\ttfamily $<$cursor down key$>$} to jump into the search results window, the results can be navigated using the {\ttfamily $<$cursor keys$>$}. Press {\ttfamily $<$Enter$>$} to select an item or {\ttfamily $<$escape$>$} to cancel the search. The filter options can be selected when the cursor is inside the search box by pressing {\ttfamily $<$Shift$>$+$<$cursor down$>$}. Also here use the {\ttfamily $<$cursor keys$>$} to select a filter and {\ttfamily $<$Enter$>$} or {\ttfamily $<$escape$>$} to activate or cancel the filter option.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_html}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+T\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_server_based_search}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_server_based_search}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH} ]\index{SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH@{SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH}} When the {\ttfamily S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH} tag is enabled the search engine will be implemented using a web server instead of a web client using Javascript.

There are two flavors of web server based searching depending on the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} setting. When disabled, doxygen will generate a P\+HP script for searching and an index file used by the script. When \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} is enabled the indexing and searching needs to be provided by external tools. See the section \mbox{\hyperlink{extsearch}{External Indexing and Searching}} for details.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_external_search}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_external_search}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH} ]\index{EXTERNAL\_SEARCH@{EXTERNAL\_SEARCH}} When {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH} tag is enabled doxygen will no longer generate the P\+HP script for searching. Instead the search results are written to an X\+ML file which needs to be processed by an external indexer. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will invoke an external search engine pointed to by the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine_url}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+U\+RL}} option to obtain the search results. ~\newline
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} ships with an example indexer ({\ttfamily doxyindexer}) and search engine ({\ttfamily doxysearch.\+cgi}) which are based on the open source search engine library \href{https://xapian.org/}{\texttt{ Xapian}}. ~\newline
See the section \mbox{\hyperlink{extsearch}{External Indexing and Searching}} for details.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_searchengine_url}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_searchengine_url}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+U\+RL} ]\index{SEARCHENGINE\_URL@{SEARCHENGINE\_URL}} The {\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+U\+RL} should point to a search engine hosted by a web server which will return the search results when \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} is enabled. ~\newline
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} ships with an example indexer ({\ttfamily doxyindexer}) and search engine ({\ttfamily doxysearch.\+cgi}) which are based on the open source search engine library \href{https://xapian.org/}{\texttt{ Xapian}}. See the section \mbox{\hyperlink{extsearch}{External Indexing and Searching}} for details.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_searchdata_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_searchdata_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{SEARCHDATA\_FILE@{SEARCHDATA\_FILE}} When \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_server_based_search}{S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} are both enabled the unindexed search data is written to a file for indexing by an external tool. With the {\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag the name of this file can be specified.

The default file is\+: {\ttfamily searchdata.\+xml}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_external_search_id}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_external_search_id}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+ID} ]\index{EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\_ID@{EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\_ID}} When \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_server_based_search}{S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+CH}} are both enabled the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+ID} tag can be used as an identifier for the project. This is useful in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_extra_search_mappings}{E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+N\+GS}} to search through multiple projects and redirect the results back to the right project.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_extra_search_mappings}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extra_search_mappings}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+N\+GS} ]\index{EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS@{EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+N\+GS} tag can be used to enable searching through doxygen projects other than the one defined by this configuration file, but that are all added to the same external search index. Each project needs to have a unique id set via \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_external_search_id}{E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+ID}}. The search mapping then maps the id of to a relative location where the documentation can be found.

The format is\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}EXTRA_SEARCH_MAPPINGS = tagname1=loc1 tagname2=loc2 ...
\end{DoxyVerb}


This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_searchengine}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+E\+N\+G\+I\+NE}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_latex}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the La\+Te\+X output}\label{config_config_latex}
\label{config_cfg_generate_latex}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_latex}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} ]\index{GENERATE\_LATEX@{GENERATE\_LATEX}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_latex_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{LATEX\_OUTPUT@{LATEX\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ docs will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily latex}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_cmd_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_cmd_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{LATEX\_CMD\_NAME@{LATEX\_CMD\_NAME}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag can be used to specify the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ command name to be invoked. ~\newline
Note that when not enabling \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_pdflatex}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+D\+F\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} the default is {\ttfamily latex} when enabling \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_use_pdflatex}{U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+D\+F\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} the default is {\ttfamily pdflatex} and when in the later case {\ttfamily latex} is chosen this is overwritten by {\ttfamily pdflatex}. For specific output languages the default can have been set differently, this depends on the implementation of the output language.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_makeindex_cmd_name}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_makeindex_cmd_name}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{MAKEINDEX\_CMD\_NAME@{MAKEINDEX\_CMD\_NAME}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME} tag can be used to specify the command name to generate index for $\mbox{\LaTeX}$.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This tag is used in the {\ttfamily Makefile} / {\ttfamily make.\+bat}. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_makeindex_cmd}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+MD}} for the part in the generated \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad41edd103217aafc3fb5613fe98b87a0}{output}} \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} ({\ttfamily .tex}).
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
The default file is\+: {\ttfamily makeindex}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_makeindex_cmd}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_makeindex_cmd}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+MD} ]\index{LATEX\_MAKEINDEX\_CMD@{LATEX\_MAKEINDEX\_CMD}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+MD} tag can be used to specify the command name to generate index for $\mbox{\LaTeX}$. In case there is no backslash ({\ttfamily \textbackslash{}}) as first character it will be automatically added in the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ code.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This tag is used in the generated output file ({\ttfamily .tex}). 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_makeindex_cmd_name}{M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}} for the part in the {\ttfamily Makefile} / {\ttfamily make.\+bat}.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily makeindex}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_compact_latex}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_compact_latex}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+P\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} ]\index{COMPACT\_LATEX@{COMPACT\_LATEX}} If the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+P\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen generates more compact $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ documents. This may be useful for small projects and may help to save some trees in general.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_paper_type}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_paper_type}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+A\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} ]\index{PAPER\_TYPE@{PAPER\_TYPE}} The {\ttfamily P\+A\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} tag can be used to set the paper type that is used by the printer.

Possible values are\+: {\ttfamily a4} (210 x 297 mm), {\ttfamily letter} (8.\+5 x 11 inches), {\ttfamily legal} (8.\+5 x 14 inches) and {\ttfamily executive} (7.\+25 x 10.\+5 inches).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily a4}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_extra_packages}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_extra_packages}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+A\+G\+ES} ]\index{EXTRA\_PACKAGES@{EXTRA\_PACKAGES}} The {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+A\+G\+ES} tag can be used to specify one or more $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ package names that should be included in the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ output. The package can be specified just by its name or with the correct syntax as to be used with the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}usepackage} command.

To get the {\ttfamily times} font for instance you can specify \+: \begin{DoxyVerb}  EXTRA_PACKAGES=times
or
  EXTRA_PACKAGES={times}
\end{DoxyVerb}
 To use the option {\ttfamily intlimits} with the {\ttfamily amsmath} package you can specify\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}   EXTRA_PACKAGES=[intlimits]{amsmath}
\end{DoxyVerb}
 If left blank no extra packages will be included.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_header}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_header}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} ]\index{LATEX\_HEADER@{LATEX\_HEADER}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} tag can be used to specify a personal $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ header for the generated $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ document. The header should contain everything until the first chapter.

If it is left blank doxygen will generate a standard header. See section \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage}{Doxygen usage}} for information on how to let doxygen write the default header to a separate file.

~\newline
Note\+: Only use a user-\/defined header if you know what you are doing!

The following commands have a special meaning inside the header\+: {\ttfamily \$title}, {\ttfamily \$datetime}, {\ttfamily \$date}, {\ttfamily \$doxygenversion}, {\ttfamily \$projectname}, {\ttfamily \$projectnumber}, {\ttfamily \$projectbrief}, {\ttfamily \$projectlogo}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will replace {\ttfamily \$title} with the empty string, for the replacement values of the other commands the user is referred to \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_header}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER}}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_footer}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_footer}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+F\+O\+O\+T\+ER} ]\index{LATEX\_FOOTER@{LATEX\_FOOTER}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+F\+O\+O\+T\+ER} tag can be used to specify a personal $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ footer for the generated $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ document. The footer should contain everything after the last chapter. If it is left blank doxygen will generate a standard footer. See \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_header}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER}} for more information on how to generate a default footer and what special commands can be used inside the footer.

~\newline
Note\+: Only use a user-\/defined footer if you know what you are doing!

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_extra_stylesheet}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_extra_stylesheet}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} ]\index{LATEX\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET@{LATEX\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+ET} tag can be used to specify additional user-\/defined $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ style sheets that are included after the standard style sheets created by doxygen. Using this option one can overrule certain style aspects. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will copy the style sheet files to the output directory. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The order of the extra style sheet files is of importance (e.\+g. the last style sheet in the list overrules the setting of the previous ones in the list).
\end{DoxyNote}
This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_extra_files}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_extra_files}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{LATEX\_EXTRA\_FILES@{LATEX\_EXTRA\_FILES}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag can be used to specify one or more extra images or other source files which should be copied to the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_output}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT}} output directory. Note that the files will be copied as-\/is; there are no commands or markers available.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_pdf_hyperlinks}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_pdf_hyperlinks}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+D\+F\+\_\+\+H\+Y\+P\+E\+R\+L\+I\+N\+KS} ]\index{PDF\_HYPERLINKS@{PDF\_HYPERLINKS}} If the {\ttfamily P\+D\+F\+\_\+\+H\+Y\+P\+E\+R\+L\+I\+N\+KS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ that is generated is prepared for conversion to P\+DF (using {\ttfamily ps2pdf} or {\ttfamily pdflatex}). The P\+DF file will contain links (just like the H\+T\+ML output) instead of page references. This makes the output suitable for online browsing using a P\+DF viewer.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_use_pdflatex}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_use_pdflatex}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+D\+F\+L\+A\+T\+EX} ]\index{USE\_PDFLATEX@{USE\_PDFLATEX}} If the {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+D\+F\+L\+A\+T\+EX} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will use {\ttfamily pdflatex} to generate the P\+DF file directly from the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ files. Set this option to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, to get a higher quality P\+DF documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_batchmode}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_batchmode}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+A\+T\+C\+H\+M\+O\+DE} ]\index{LATEX\_BATCHMODE@{LATEX\_BATCHMODE}} If the {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+A\+T\+C\+H\+M\+O\+DE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will add the {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}batchmode} command to the generated $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ files. This will instruct $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ to keep running if errors occur, instead of asking the user for help. This option is also used when generating formulas in H\+T\+ML.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_hide_indices}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_hide_indices}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+ES} ]\index{LATEX\_HIDE\_INDICES@{LATEX\_HIDE\_INDICES}} If the {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will not include the index chapters (such as File Index, Compound Index, etc.) in the output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_source_code}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_source_code}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE} ]\index{LATEX\_SOURCE\_CODE@{LATEX\_SOURCE\_CODE}} If the {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will include source code with syntax highlighting in the $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ output. ~\newline
Note that which sources are shown also depends on other settings such as \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_bib_style}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_bib_style}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+LE} ]\index{LATEX\_BIB\_STYLE@{LATEX\_BIB\_STYLE}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+LE} tag can be used to specify the style to use for the bibliography, e.\+g. {\ttfamily plainnat}, or {\ttfamily ieeetr}. See \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BibTeX}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+Bib\+TeX}} and \textbackslash{}cite for more info.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily plain}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_timestamp}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_timestamp}%

\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+MP} ]\index{LATEX\_TIMESTAMP@{LATEX\_TIMESTAMP}} If the {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+MP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the footer of each generated page will contain the date and time when the page was generated. Setting this to {\ttfamily NO} can help when comparing the output of multiple runs.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_latex_emoji_directory}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_latex_emoji_directory}%
