\item[{\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+M\+O\+J\+I\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY} ]\index{LATEX\_EMOJI\_DIRECTORY@{LATEX\_EMOJI\_DIRECTORY}} The {\ttfamily L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+E\+M\+O\+J\+I\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY} tag is used to specify the (relative or absolute) path from which the emoji images will be read. If a relative path is entered, it will be relative to the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_output}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT}} directory. If left blank the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_latex_output}{L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT}} directory will be used.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_latex}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_rtf}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the R\+T\+F output}\label{config_config_rtf}
\label{config_cfg_generate_rtf}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_rtf}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF} ]\index{GENERATE\_RTF@{GENERATE\_RTF}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate R\+TF output. The R\+TF output is optimized for Word 97 and may not look too pretty with other R\+TF readers/editors.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_rtf_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_rtf_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{RTF\_OUTPUT@{RTF\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the R\+TF docs will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily rtf}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_compact_rtf}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_compact_rtf}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+P\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+R\+TF} ]\index{COMPACT\_RTF@{COMPACT\_RTF}} If the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+P\+A\+C\+T\+\_\+\+R\+TF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen generates more compact R\+TF documents. This may be useful for small projects and may help to save some trees in general.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_rtf_hyperlinks}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_rtf_hyperlinks}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+H\+Y\+P\+E\+R\+L\+I\+N\+KS} ]\index{RTF\_HYPERLINKS@{RTF\_HYPERLINKS}} If the {\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+H\+Y\+P\+E\+R\+L\+I\+N\+KS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the R\+TF that is generated will contain hyperlink fields. The R\+TF file will contain links (just like the H\+T\+ML output) instead of page references. This makes the output suitable for online browsing using Word or some other Word compatible readers that support those fields.

~\newline
Note\+: Word\+Pad (write) and others do not support links.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_rtf_stylesheet_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_rtf_stylesheet_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+L\+E\+S\+H\+E\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{RTF\_STYLESHEET\_FILE@{RTF\_STYLESHEET\_FILE}} Load stylesheet definitions from file. Syntax is similar to doxygen\textquotesingle{}s configuration file, i.\+e. a series of assignments. You only have to provide replacements, missing definitions are set to their default value. ~\newline
 See also section \mbox{\hyperlink{doxygen_usage}{Doxygen usage}} for information on how to generate the default style sheet that doxygen normally uses.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_rtf_extensions_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_rtf_extensions_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{RTF\_EXTENSIONS\_FILE@{RTF\_EXTENSIONS\_FILE}} Set optional variables used in the generation of an R\+TF document. Syntax is similar to doxygen\textquotesingle{}s configuration file. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} template extensions file can be generated using {\ttfamily doxygen -\/e rtf extension\+File}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_rtf_source_code}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_rtf_source_code}%

\item[{\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE} ]\index{RTF\_SOURCE\_CODE@{RTF\_SOURCE\_CODE}} If the {\ttfamily R\+T\+F\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will include source code with syntax highlighting in the R\+TF output. ~\newline
Note that which sources are shown also depends on other settings such as \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_source_browser}{S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+W\+S\+ER}}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_rtf}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+TF}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_man}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the man page output}\label{config_config_man}
\label{config_cfg_generate_man}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_man}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN} ]\index{GENERATE\_MAN@{GENERATE\_MAN}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate man pages for classes and files.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_man_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_man_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{MAN\_OUTPUT@{MAN\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the man pages will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} directory {\ttfamily man3} will be created inside the directory specified by {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT}.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily man}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_man}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_man_extension}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_man_extension}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} ]\index{MAN\_EXTENSION@{MAN\_EXTENSION}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} tag determines the extension that is added to the generated man pages. In case the manual section does not start with a number, the number 3 is prepended. The dot (.) at the beginning of the {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} tag is optional.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily .3}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_man}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_man_subdir}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_man_subdir}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+D\+IR} ]\index{MAN\_SUBDIR@{MAN\_SUBDIR}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+D\+IR} tag determines the name of the directory created within {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} in which the man pages are placed. If defaults to man followed by {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON} with the initial . removed.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_man}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_man_links}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_man_links}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+KS} ]\index{MAN\_LINKS@{MAN\_LINKS}} If the {\ttfamily M\+A\+N\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+KS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} and doxygen generates man output, then it will generate one additional man file for each entity documented in the real man page(s). These additional files only source the real man page, but without them the {\ttfamily man} command would be unable to find the correct page.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_man}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+AN}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_xml}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the X\+M\+L output}\label{config_config_xml}
\label{config_cfg_generate_xml}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_xml}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+X\+ML} ]\index{GENERATE\_XML@{GENERATE\_XML}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+X\+ML} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate an X\+ML file that captures the structure of the code including all documentation.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_xml_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_xml_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{XML\_OUTPUT@{XML\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the X\+ML pages will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily xml}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_xml}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+X\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_xml_programlisting}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_xml_programlisting}%

\item[{\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+A\+M\+L\+I\+S\+T\+I\+NG} ]\index{XML\_PROGRAMLISTING@{XML\_PROGRAMLISTING}} If the {\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+A\+M\+L\+I\+S\+T\+I\+NG} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will dump the program listings (including syntax highlighting and cross-\/referencing information) to the X\+ML output. Note that enabling this will significantly increase the size of the X\+ML output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_xml}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+X\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_xml_ns_memb_file_scope}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_xml_ns_memb_file_scope}%

\item[{\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+N\+S\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+PE} ]\index{XML\_NS\_MEMB\_FILE\_SCOPE@{XML\_NS\_MEMB\_FILE\_SCOPE}} If the {\ttfamily X\+M\+L\+\_\+\+N\+S\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+PE} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will include namespace members in file scope as well, matching the H\+T\+ML output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_xml}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+X\+ML}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_docbook}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+O\+K output}\label{config_config_docbook}
\label{config_cfg_generate_docbook}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_docbook}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK} ]\index{GENERATE\_DOCBOOK@{GENERATE\_DOCBOOK}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate Docbook files that can be used to generate P\+DF.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_docbook_output}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docbook_output}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} ]\index{DOCBOOK\_OUTPUT@{DOCBOOK\_OUTPUT}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+UT} tag is used to specify where the Docbook pages will be put. If a relative path is entered the value of \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_output_directory}{O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RY}} will be put in front of it.

The default directory is\+: {\ttfamily docbook}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docbook}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_docbook_programlisting}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_docbook_programlisting}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+A\+M\+L\+I\+S\+T\+I\+NG} ]\index{DOCBOOK\_PROGRAMLISTING@{DOCBOOK\_PROGRAMLISTING}} If the {\ttfamily D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+A\+M\+L\+I\+S\+T\+I\+NG} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will include the program listings (including syntax highlighting and cross-\/referencing information) to the D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK output. Note that enabling this will significantly increase the size of the D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_docbook}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+O\+C\+B\+O\+OK}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_autogen}{}\doxysection{Configuration options for the Auto\+Gen Definitions output}\label{config_config_autogen}
\label{config_cfg_generate_autogen_def}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_autogen_def}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+G\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+EF} ]\index{GENERATE\_AUTOGEN\_DEF@{GENERATE\_AUTOGEN\_DEF}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+G\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+EF} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate an Auto\+Gen Definitions (see \href{http://autogen.sourceforge.net/}{\texttt{ http\+://autogen.\+sourceforge.\+net/}}) file that captures the structure of the code including all documentation. Note that this feature is still experimental and incomplete at the moment.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_perlmod}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the Perl module output}\label{config_config_perlmod}
\label{config_cfg_generate_perlmod}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_perlmod}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+OD} ]\index{GENERATE\_PERLMOD@{GENERATE\_PERLMOD}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+OD} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate a Perl module file that captures the structure of the code including all documentation. ~\newline
Note that this feature is still experimental and incomplete at the moment.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_perlmod_latex}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_perlmod_latex}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} ]\index{PERLMOD\_LATEX@{PERLMOD\_LATEX}} If the {\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+EX} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate the necessary {\ttfamily Makefile} rules, {\ttfamily Perl} scripts and $\mbox{\LaTeX}$ code to be able to generate P\+DF and D\+VI output from the Perl module output.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_perlmod}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+OD}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_perlmod_pretty}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_perlmod_pretty}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+T\+TY} ]\index{PERLMOD\_PRETTY@{PERLMOD\_PRETTY}} If the {\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+T\+TY} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the Perl module output will be nicely formatted so it can be parsed by a human reader. This is useful if you want to understand what is going on. On the other hand, if this tag is set to {\ttfamily NO}, the size of the Perl module output will be much smaller and Perl will parse it just the same.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_perlmod}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+OD}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_perlmod_makevar_prefix}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_perlmod_makevar_prefix}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+M\+A\+K\+E\+V\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+F\+IX} ]\index{PERLMOD\_MAKEVAR\_PREFIX@{PERLMOD\_MAKEVAR\_PREFIX}} The names of the make variables in the generated {\ttfamily doxyrules.\+make} file are prefixed with the string contained in {\ttfamily P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+O\+D\+\_\+\+M\+A\+K\+E\+V\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+F\+IX}. This is useful so different {\ttfamily doxyrules.\+make} files included by the same {\ttfamily Makefile} don\textquotesingle{}t overwrite each other\textquotesingle{}s variables.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_generate_perlmod}{G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+L\+M\+OD}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_preprocessor}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the preprocessor}\label{config_config_preprocessor}
\label{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG} ]\index{ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING@{ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING}} If the {\ttfamily E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will evaluate all C-\/preprocessor directives found in the sources and include files.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_macro_expansion}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_macro_expansion}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+C\+R\+O\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+ON} ]\index{MACRO\_EXPANSION@{MACRO\_EXPANSION}} If the {\ttfamily M\+A\+C\+R\+O\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+ON} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will expand all macro names in the source code. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only conditional compilation will be performed. Macro expansion can be done in a controlled way by setting \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_expand_only_predef}{E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+D\+EF}} to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_expand_only_predef}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_expand_only_predef}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+D\+EF} ]\index{EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF@{EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+D\+EF} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_macro_expansion}{M\+A\+C\+R\+O\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+ON}} tags are both set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the macro expansion is limited to the macros specified with the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_predefined}{P\+R\+E\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_expand_as_defined}{E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}} tags.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_search_includes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_search_includes}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES} ]\index{SEARCH\_INCLUDES@{SEARCH\_INCLUDES}} If the {\ttfamily S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, the include files in the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_include_path}{I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}} will be searched if a {\ttfamily \#include} is found.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_include_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_include_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{INCLUDE\_PATH@{INCLUDE\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to specify one or more directories that contain include files that are not input files but should be processed by the preprocessor.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_search_includes}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_include_file_patterns}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_include_file_patterns}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} ]\index{INCLUDE\_FILE\_PATTERNS@{INCLUDE\_FILE\_PATTERNS}} You can use the {\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS} tag to specify one or more wildcard patterns (like {\ttfamily $\ast$.h} and {\ttfamily $\ast$.hpp}) to filter out the header-\/files in the directories. If left blank, the patterns specified with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_file_patterns}{F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+T\+E\+R\+NS}} will be used.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_predefined}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_predefined}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+R\+E\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED} ]\index{PREDEFINED@{PREDEFINED}} The {\ttfamily P\+R\+E\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED} tag can be used to specify one or more macro names that are defined before the preprocessor is started (similar to the {\ttfamily -\/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_d}{D}}} option of e.\+g. {\ttfamily gcc}). The argument of the tag is a list of macros of the form\+: {\ttfamily name} or {\ttfamily name=definition} (no spaces). If the definition and the {\ttfamily \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}} are omitted, {\ttfamily \char`\"{}=1\char`\"{}} is assumed. To prevent a macro definition from being undefined via {\ttfamily \#undef} or recursively expanded use the {\ttfamily \+:=} operator instead of the {\ttfamily =} operator.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_expand_as_defined}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_expand_as_defined}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED} ]\index{EXPAND\_AS\_DEFINED@{EXPAND\_AS\_DEFINED}} If the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_macro_expansion}{M\+A\+C\+R\+O\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+ON}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_expand_only_predef}{E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+D\+EF}} tags are set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then this tag can be used to specify a list of macro names that should be expanded. The macro definition that is found in the sources will be used. Use the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_predefined}{P\+R\+E\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}} tag if you want to use a different macro definition that overrules the definition found in the source code.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_skip_function_macros}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_skip_function_macros}%

\item[{\ttfamily S\+K\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+U\+N\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+R\+OS} ]\index{SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS@{SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS}} If the {\ttfamily S\+K\+I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+U\+N\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+R\+OS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen\textquotesingle{}s preprocessor will remove all references to function-\/like macros that are alone on a line, have an all uppercase name, and do not end with a semicolon. Such function macros are typically used for boiler-\/plate code, and will confuse the parser if not removed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_external}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to external references}\label{config_config_external}
\label{config_cfg_tagfiles}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_tagfiles}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily T\+A\+G\+F\+I\+L\+ES} ]\index{TAGFILES@{TAGFILES}} The {\ttfamily T\+A\+G\+F\+I\+L\+ES} tag can be used to specify one or more tag files.

For each tag file the location of the external documentation should be added. The format of a tag file without this location is as follows\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}  TAGFILES = file1 file2 ...
\end{DoxyVerb}
 Adding location for the tag files is done as follows\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}  TAGFILES = file1=loc1 "file2 = loc2" ...
\end{DoxyVerb}
 where {\ttfamily loc1} and {\ttfamily loc2} can be relative or absolute paths or U\+R\+Ls. See the section \mbox{\hyperlink{external}{Linking to external documentation}} for more information about the use of tag files.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Each tag file must have a unique name (where the name does {\itshape N\+OT} include the path). If a tag file is not located in the directory in which doxygen is run, you must also specify the path to the tagfile here.
\end{DoxyNote}
\label{config_cfg_generate_tagfile}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_tagfile}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+A\+G\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{GENERATE\_TAGFILE@{GENERATE\_TAGFILE}} When a file name is specified after {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+A\+G\+F\+I\+LE}, doxygen will create a tag file that is based on the input files it reads. See section \mbox{\hyperlink{external}{Linking to external documentation}} for more information about the usage of tag files.

\label{config_cfg_allexternals}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_allexternals}%

\item[{\ttfamily A\+L\+L\+E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+LS} ]\index{ALLEXTERNALS@{ALLEXTERNALS}} If the {\ttfamily A\+L\+L\+E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+LS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all external class will be listed in the class index. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only the inherited external classes will be listed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_external_groups}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_external_groups}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+PS} ]\index{EXTERNAL\_GROUPS@{EXTERNAL\_GROUPS}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+PS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all external groups will be listed in the modules index. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only the current project\textquotesingle{}s groups will be listed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_external_pages}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_external_pages}%

\item[{\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES} ]\index{EXTERNAL\_PAGES@{EXTERNAL\_PAGES}} If the {\ttfamily E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, all external pages will be listed in the related pages index. If set to {\ttfamily NO}, only the current project\textquotesingle{}s pages will be listed.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.


\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_dot}{}\doxysection{Configuration options related to the dot tool}\label{config_config_dot}
\label{config_cfg_class_diagrams}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_class_diagrams}%

\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[{\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+G\+R\+A\+MS} ]\index{CLASS\_DIAGRAMS@{CLASS\_DIAGRAMS}} If the {\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+G\+R\+A\+MS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate a class diagram (in H\+T\+ML and $\mbox{\LaTeX}$) for classes with base or super classes. Setting the tag to {\ttfamily NO} turns the diagrams off. Note that this option also works with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} disabled, but it is recommended to install and use {\ttfamily dot}, since it yields more powerful graphs.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_dia_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dia_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{DIA\_PATH@{DIA\_PATH}} You can include diagrams made with dia in doxygen documentation. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will then run dia to produce the diagram and insert it in the documentation. The D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH tag allows you to specify the directory where the dia binary resides. If left empty dia is assumed to be found in the default search path.

\label{config_cfg_hide_undoc_relations}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_hide_undoc_relations}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+O\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{HIDE\_UNDOC\_RELATIONS@{HIDE\_UNDOC\_RELATIONS}} If set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} the inheritance and collaboration graphs will hide inheritance and usage relations if the target is undocumented or is not a class.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

\label{config_cfg_have_dot}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_have_dot}%

\item[{\ttfamily H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT} ]\index{HAVE\_DOT@{HAVE\_DOT}} If you set the {\ttfamily H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will assume the {\ttfamily dot} tool is available from the {\ttfamily path}. This tool is part of \href{http://www.graphviz.org/}{\texttt{ Graphviz}}, a graph visualization toolkit from AT\&T and Lucent Bell Labs. The other options in this section have no effect if this option is set to {\ttfamily NO} 

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

\label{config_cfg_dot_num_threads}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_num_threads}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+DS} ]\index{DOT\_NUM\_THREADS@{DOT\_NUM\_THREADS}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+DS} specifies the number of {\ttfamily dot} invocations doxygen is allowed to run in parallel. When set to {\ttfamily 0} doxygen will base this on the number of processors available in the system. You can set it explicitly to a value larger than 0 to get control over the balance between C\+PU load and processing speed.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 32}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 0}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_fontname}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_fontname}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+N\+A\+ME} ]\index{DOT\_FONTNAME@{DOT\_FONTNAME}} When you want a differently looking font in the dot files that doxygen generates you can specify the font name using {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+N\+A\+ME}. You need to make sure dot is able to find the font, which can be done by putting it in a standard location or by setting the {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+F\+O\+N\+T\+P\+A\+TH} environment variable or by setting \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_dot_fontpath}{D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+P\+A\+TH}} to the directory containing the font.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Helvetica}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_fontsize}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_fontsize}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+S\+I\+ZE} ]\index{DOT\_FONTSIZE@{DOT\_FONTSIZE}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+S\+I\+ZE} tag can be used to set the size (in points) of the font of dot graphs.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 4}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 24}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 10}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_fontpath}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_fontpath}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{DOT\_FONTPATH@{DOT\_FONTPATH}} By default doxygen will tell {\ttfamily dot} to use the default font as specified with \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_dot_fontname}{D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+N\+A\+ME}}. If you specify a different font using \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_dot_fontname}{D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+N\+T\+N\+A\+ME}} you can set the path where {\ttfamily dot} can find it using this tag.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_class_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_class_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{CLASS\_GRAPH@{CLASS\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a graph for each documented class showing the direct and indirect inheritance relations. Setting this tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} will force the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_class_diagrams}{C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+G\+R\+A\+MS}} tag to {\ttfamily NO}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_collaboration_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_collaboration_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+O\+L\+L\+A\+B\+O\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{COLLABORATION\_GRAPH@{COLLABORATION\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily C\+O\+L\+L\+A\+B\+O\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a graph for each documented class showing the direct and indirect implementation dependencies (inheritance, containment, and class references variables) of the class with other documented classes.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_group_graphs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_group_graphs}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+HS} ]\index{GROUP\_GRAPHS@{GROUP\_GRAPHS}} If the {\ttfamily G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+HS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a graph for groups, showing the direct groups dependencies.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_uml_look}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_uml_look}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+O\+OK} ]\index{UML\_LOOK@{UML\_LOOK}} If the {\ttfamily U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+O\+OK} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will generate inheritance and collaboration diagrams in a style similar to the O\+MG\textquotesingle{}s Unified Modeling Language.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_uml_limit_num_fields}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_uml_limit_num_fields}%

\item[{\ttfamily U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+I\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+F\+I\+E\+L\+DS} ]\index{UML\_LIMIT\_NUM\_FIELDS@{UML\_LIMIT\_NUM\_FIELDS}} If the \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_uml_look}{U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+O\+OK}} tag is enabled, the fields and methods are shown inside the class node. If there are many fields or methods and many nodes the graph may become too big to be useful. The {\ttfamily U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+I\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+F\+I\+E\+L\+DS} threshold limits the number of items for each type to make the size more manageable. Set this to 0 for no limit. Note that the threshold may be exceeded by 50\% before the limit is enforced. So when you set the threshold to 10, up to 15 fields may appear, but if the number exceeds 15, the total amount of fields shown is limited to 10.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 100}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 10}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_template_relations}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_template_relations}%

\item[{\ttfamily T\+E\+M\+P\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+O\+NS} ]\index{TEMPLATE\_RELATIONS@{TEMPLATE\_RELATIONS}} If the {\ttfamily T\+E\+M\+P\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+A\+T\+I\+O\+NS} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then the inheritance and collaboration graphs will show the relations between templates and their instances.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_include_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_include_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{INCLUDE\_GRAPH@{INCLUDE\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH}, \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_search_includes}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES}} tags are set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a graph for each documented file showing the direct and indirect include dependencies of the file with other documented files.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_included_by_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_included_by_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{INCLUDED\_BY\_GRAPH@{INCLUDED\_BY\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH}, \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_enable_preprocessing}{E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+I\+NG}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_search_includes}{S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+ES}} tags are set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a graph for each documented file showing the direct and indirect include dependencies of the file with other documented files.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_call_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_call_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{CALL\_GRAPH@{CALL\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a call dependency graph for every global function or class method. ~\newline
Note that enabling this option will significantly increase the time of a run. So in most cases it will be better to enable call graphs for selected functions only using the \textbackslash{}callgraph command. Disabling a call graph can be accomplished by means of the command \textbackslash{}hidecallgraph.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_caller_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_caller_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily C\+A\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{CALLER\_GRAPH@{CALLER\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily C\+A\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will generate a caller dependency graph for every global function or class method. ~\newline
Note that enabling this option will significantly increase the time of a run. So in most cases it will be better to enable caller graphs for selected functions only using the \textbackslash{}callergraph command. Disabling a caller graph can be accomplished by means of the command \textbackslash{}hidecallergraph.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_graphical_hierarchy}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_graphical_hierarchy}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+E\+R\+A\+R\+C\+HY} ]\index{GRAPHICAL\_HIERARCHY@{GRAPHICAL\_HIERARCHY}} If the {\ttfamily G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+E\+R\+A\+R\+C\+HY} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will graphical hierarchy of all classes instead of a textual one.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_directory_graph}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_directory_graph}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} ]\index{DIRECTORY\_GRAPH@{DIRECTORY\_GRAPH}} If the {\ttfamily D\+I\+R\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+PH} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} then doxygen will show the dependencies a directory has on other directories in a graphical way. The dependency relations are determined by the {\ttfamily \#include} relations between the files in the directories.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_image_format}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_image_format}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT} ]\index{DOT\_IMAGE\_FORMAT@{DOT\_IMAGE\_FORMAT}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT} tag can be used to set the image format of the images generated by {\ttfamily dot}. For an explanation of the image formats see the section output formats in the documentation of the {\ttfamily dot} tool (\href{http://www.graphviz.org/}{\texttt{ Graphviz}}). \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you choose {\ttfamily svg} you need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_file_extension}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON}} to {\ttfamily xhtml} in order to make the S\+VG files visible in IE 9+ (other browsers do not have this requirement).
\end{DoxyNote}
Possible values are\+: {\ttfamily png}, {\ttfamily jpg}, {\ttfamily gif}, {\ttfamily svg}, {\ttfamily png\+:gd}, {\ttfamily png\+:gd\+:gd}, {\ttfamily png\+:cairo}, {\ttfamily png\+:cairo\+:gd}, {\ttfamily png\+:cairo\+:cairo}, {\ttfamily png\+:cairo\+:gdiplus}, {\ttfamily png\+:gdiplus} and {\ttfamily png\+:gdiplus\+:gdiplus}.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily png}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_interactive_svg}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_interactive_svg}%

\item[{\ttfamily I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+S\+VG} ]\index{INTERACTIVE\_SVG@{INTERACTIVE\_SVG}} If \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_dot_image_format}{D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT}} is set to {\ttfamily svg}, then this option can be set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to enable generation of interactive S\+VG images that allow zooming and panning. ~\newline
Note that this requires a modern browser other than Internet Explorer. Tested and working are Firefox, Chrome, Safari, and Opera. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For IE 9+ you need to set \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_html_file_extension}{H\+T\+M\+L\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+ON}} to {\ttfamily xhtml} in order to make the S\+VG files visible. Older versions of IE do not have S\+VG support.
\end{DoxyNote}
The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{DOT\_PATH@{DOT\_PATH}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag can be used to specify the path where the {\ttfamily dot} tool can be found. If left blank, it is assumed the {\ttfamily dot} tool can be found in the {\ttfamily path}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dotfile_dirs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dotfile_dirs}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} ]\index{DOTFILE\_DIRS@{DOTFILE\_DIRS}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} tag can be used to specify one or more directories that contain dot files that are included in the documentation (see the \textbackslash{}dotfile command).

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_mscfile_dirs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_mscfile_dirs}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+S\+C\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} ]\index{MSCFILE\_DIRS@{MSCFILE\_DIRS}} The {\ttfamily M\+S\+C\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} tag can be used to specify one or more directories that contain msc files that are included in the documentation (see the \textbackslash{}mscfile command).

\label{config_cfg_diafile_dirs}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_diafile_dirs}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+I\+A\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} ]\index{DIAFILE\_DIRS@{DIAFILE\_DIRS}} The {\ttfamily D\+I\+A\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+RS} tag can be used to specify one or more directories that contain dia files that are included in the documentation (see the \textbackslash{}diafile command).

\label{config_cfg_plantuml_jar_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_plantuml_jar_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+L\+A\+N\+T\+U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+J\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{PLANTUML\_JAR\_PATH@{PLANTUML\_JAR\_PATH}} When using plantuml, the {\ttfamily P\+L\+A\+N\+T\+U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+J\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} tag should be used to specify the path where java can find the {\ttfamily plantuml.\+jar} file. If left blank, it is assumed Plant\+U\+ML is not used or called during a preprocessing step. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} will generate a warning when it encounters a \textbackslash{}startuml command in this case and will not generate output for the diagram.

\label{config_cfg_plantuml_cfg_file}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_plantuml_cfg_file}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+L\+A\+N\+T\+U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+F\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} ]\index{PLANTUML\_CFG\_FILE@{PLANTUML\_CFG\_FILE}} When using plantuml, the {\ttfamily P\+L\+A\+N\+T\+U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+C\+F\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE} tag can be used to specify a configuration file for plantuml.

\label{config_cfg_plantuml_include_path}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_plantuml_include_path}%

\item[{\ttfamily P\+L\+A\+N\+T\+U\+M\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH} ]\index{PLANTUML\_INCLUDE\_PATH@{PLANTUML\_INCLUDE\_PATH}} When using plantuml, the specified paths are searched for files specified by the {\ttfamily !include} statement in a plantuml block.

\label{config_cfg_dot_graph_max_nodes}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_graph_max_nodes}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+ES} ]\index{DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES@{DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES}} The {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+ES} tag can be used to set the maximum number of nodes that will be shown in the graph. If the number of nodes in a graph becomes larger than this value, doxygen will truncate the graph, which is visualized by representing a node as a red box. Note that doxygen if the number of direct children of the root node in a graph is already larger than {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+ES} then the graph will not be shown at all. Also note that the size of a graph can be further restricted by \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_max_dot_graph_depth}{M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+TH}}.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 10000}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 50}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_max_dot_graph_depth}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_max_dot_graph_depth}%

\item[{\ttfamily M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+TH} ]\index{MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH@{MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH}} The {\ttfamily M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+TH} tag can be used to set the maximum depth of the graphs generated by {\ttfamily dot}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} depth value of 3 means that only nodes reachable from the root by following a path via at most 3 edges will be shown. Nodes that lay further from the root node will be omitted. Note that setting this option to 1 or 2 may greatly reduce the computation time needed for large code bases. Also note that the size of a graph can be further restricted by \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_dot_graph_max_nodes}{D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+ES}}. Using a depth of 0 means no depth restriction.

Minimum value\+: {\ttfamily 0}, maximum value\+: {\ttfamily 1000}, default value\+: {\ttfamily 0}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_transparent}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_transparent}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+A\+R\+E\+NT} ]\index{DOT\_TRANSPARENT@{DOT\_TRANSPARENT}} Set the {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+A\+R\+E\+NT} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to generate images with a transparent background. This is disabled by default, because dot on Windows does not seem to support this out of the box. ~\newline
 Warning\+: Depending on the platform used, enabling this option may lead to badly anti-\/aliased labels on the edges of a graph (i.\+e. they become hard to read).

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_multi_targets}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_multi_targets}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+TS} ]\index{DOT\_MULTI\_TARGETS@{DOT\_MULTI\_TARGETS}} Set the {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+TS} tag to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} to allow dot to generate multiple output files in one run (i.\+e. multiple -\/o and -\/T options on the command line). This makes {\ttfamily dot} run faster, but since only newer versions of {\ttfamily dot} ($>$1.\+8.\+10) support this, this feature is disabled by default.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily NO}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_generate_legend}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_generate_legend}%

\item[{\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+E\+ND} ]\index{GENERATE\_LEGEND@{GENERATE\_LEGEND}} If the {\ttfamily G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+E\+ND} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES} doxygen will generate a legend page explaining the meaning of the various boxes and arrows in the dot generated graphs.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. \label{config_cfg_dot_cleanup}%
\Hypertarget{config_cfg_dot_cleanup}%

\item[{\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+E\+A\+N\+UP} ]\index{DOT\_CLEANUP@{DOT\_CLEANUP}} If the {\ttfamily D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+E\+A\+N\+UP} tag is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}, doxygen will remove the intermediate dot files that are used to generate the various graphs.

The default value is\+: {\ttfamily Y\+ES}.

This tag requires that the tag \mbox{\hyperlink{config_cfg_have_dot}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+D\+OT}} is set to {\ttfamily Y\+ES}. 
\end{DoxyDescription}\hypertarget{config_config_examples}{}\doxysection{Examples}\label{config_config_examples}
Suppose you have a simple project consisting of two files\+: a source file {\ttfamily example.\+cc} and a header file {\ttfamily example.\+h}. Then a minimal configuration file is as simple as\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}INPUT            = example.cc example.h
\end{DoxyVerb}


Assuming the example makes use of Qt classes and {\ttfamily perl} is located in {\ttfamily /usr/bin}, a more realistic configuration file would be\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}PROJECT_NAME     = Example
INPUT            = example.cc example.h
WARNINGS         = YES
TAGFILES         = qt.tag
SEARCHENGINE     = NO
\end{DoxyVerb}


To generate the documentation for the \href{https://sourceforge.net/projects/qdbttabular/}{\texttt{ Qdbt\+Tabular}} package I have used the following configuration file\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}PROJECT_NAME     = QdbtTabular
OUTPUT_DIRECTORY = html
WARNINGS         = YES
INPUT            = examples/examples.doc src
FILE_PATTERNS    = *.cc *.h
INCLUDE_PATH     = examples
TAGFILES         = qt.tag
SEARCHENGINE     = YES
\end{DoxyVerb}


To regenerate the Qt-\/1.\+44 documentation from the sources, you could use the following configuration file\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}PROJECT_NAME         = Qt
OUTPUT_DIRECTORY     = qt_docs
HIDE_UNDOC_MEMBERS   = YES
HIDE_UNDOC_CLASSES   = YES
ENABLE_PREPROCESSING = YES
MACRO_EXPANSION      = YES
EXPAND_ONLY_PREDEF   = YES
SEARCH_INCLUDES      = YES
FULL_PATH_NAMES      = YES
STRIP_FROM_PATH      = $(QTDIR)/
PREDEFINED           = USE_TEMPLATECLASS Q_EXPORT= \
                       QArrayT:=QArray \
                       QListT:=QList \
                       QDictT:=QDict \
                       QQueueT:=QQueue \
                       QVectorT:=QVector \
                       QPtrDictT:=QPtrDict \
                       QIntDictT:=QIntDict \
                       QStackT:=QStack \
                       QDictIteratorT:=QDictIterator \
                       QListIteratorT:=QListIterator \
                       QCacheT:=QCache \
                       QCacheIteratorT:=QCacheIterator \
                       QIntCacheT:=QIntCache \
                       QIntCacheIteratorT:=QIntCacheIterator \
                       QIntDictIteratorT:=QIntDictIterator \
                       QPtrDictIteratorT:=QPtrDictIterator
INPUT                = $(QTDIR)/doc \
                       $(QTDIR)/src/widgets \
                       $(QTDIR)/src/kernel \
                       $(QTDIR)/src/dialogs \
                       $(QTDIR)/src/tools
FILE_PATTERNS        = *.cpp *.h q*.doc
INCLUDE_PATH         = $(QTDIR)/include
RECURSIVE            = YES
\end{DoxyVerb}


For the Qt-\/2.\+1 sources I recommend to use the following settings\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}PROJECT_NAME          = Qt
PROJECT_NUMBER        = 2.1
HIDE_UNDOC_MEMBERS    = YES
HIDE_UNDOC_CLASSES    = YES
SOURCE_BROWSER        = YES
INPUT                 = $(QTDIR)/src
FILE_PATTERNS         = *.cpp *.h q*.doc
RECURSIVE             = YES
EXCLUDE_PATTERNS      = *codec.cpp moc_* */compat/* */3rdparty/*
ALPHABETICAL_INDEX    = YES
COLS_IN_ALPHA_INDEX   = 3
IGNORE_PREFIX         = Q
ENABLE_PREPROCESSING  = YES
MACRO_EXPANSION       = YES
INCLUDE_PATH          = $(QTDIR)/include
PREDEFINED            = Q_PROPERTY(x)= \
                        Q_OVERRIDE(x)= \
                        Q_EXPORT= \
                        Q_ENUMS(x)= \
                        "QT_STATIC_CONST=static const " \
                        _WS_X11_ \
                        INCLUDE_MENUITEM_DEF
EXPAND_ONLY_PREDEF    = YES
EXPAND_AS_DEFINED     = Q_OBJECT_FAKE Q_OBJECT ACTIVATE_SIGNAL_WITH_PARAM \
                        Q_VARIANT_AS
\end{DoxyVerb}


Here doxygen\textquotesingle{}s preprocessor is used to substitute some macro names that are normally substituted by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}} preprocessor, but without doing full macro expansion.
